  84вҶ’def main() -> None:
  85вҶ’    args = parse_args()
  86вҶ’
  87вҶ’    # 1. еҲқе§ӢеҢ–ж—Ҙеҝ—пјҲжңҖе…Ҳжү§иЎҢпјү
  88вҶ’    from mytrader.monitor.logger_setup import setup_logger
  89вҶ’    setup_logger(log_dir=args.log_dir, level="INFO")
  90вҶ’
  91вҶ’    from loguru import logger
  92вҶ’    logger.info(f"MyTrader starting: mode={args.mode or 'from_config'} dry_run={args.dry_run}")
  93вҶ’
  94вҶ’    # 2. еҠ иҪҪй…ҚзҪ®
  95вҶ’    from mytrader.infra.config import load_config
  96вҶ’    config = load_config(args.config)
  97вҶ’
  98вҶ’    # CLI --mode иҰҶзӣ–й…ҚзҪ®ж–Үд»¶
  99вҶ’    if args.mode is not None:
 100вҶ’        object.__setattr__(config.execution, "mode", args.mode)
 101вҶ’        logger.info(f"Execution mode overridden by CLI: {args.mode}")
 102вҶ’
 103вҶ’    logger.info(
 104вҶ’        f"Config loaded: mode={config.execution.mode} broker={config.execution.broker} "
 105вҶ’        f"scheduler.enabled={config.scheduler.enabled} "
 106вҶ’        f"watchlist={config.watchlist.symbols}"
 107вҶ’    )
 108вҶ’
 109вҶ’    # 3. иЈ…й…Қдҫқиө–
 110вҶ’    from mytrader.infra.container import Container
 111вҶ’    components = Container.build(config, db_url=f"sqlite:///{args.db}")
 112вҶ’
 113вҶ’    # 4. еҒҘеә·жЈҖжҹҘ
 114вҶ’    report = components.health.run_all()
 115вҶ’    logger.info(f"Health check: {report.status} ({report.checks})")
 116вҶ’    if not report.is_healthy:
 117вҶ’        for name in report.failed_checks:
 118вҶ’            logger.warning(f"Health check FAILED: {name} вҖ” {report.details.get(name)}")
 119вҶ’
 120вҶ’    # 5. жһ„е»әжү«жҸҸзј–жҺ’еҷЁ

 122вҶ’    orchestrator = build_orchestrator(components)
 123вҶ’
 124вҶ’    mode_label = "Phase 5 (multi-strategy matrix)" if orchestrator._use_phase5 else "Phase 4 (single-strategy)"
 125вҶ’    logger.info(f"[Orchestrator] Built in {mode_label} mode")
 126вҶ’
 127вҶ’    # 6a. --backfillпјҡйҰ–ж¬ЎеӣһеЎ«еҺҶеҸІж•°жҚ®
 128вҶ’    if args.backfill:
 129вҶ’        _run_backfill(config, logger)
 130вҶ’        return
 131вҶ’
 132вҶ’    # 6b. --reoptimizeпјҡз«ӢеҚіи§ҰеҸ‘ MatrixBacktest
 133вҶ’    if args.reoptimize:
 134вҶ’        _run_reoptimize(config, logger)
 135вҶ’        return
 136вҶ’
 137вҶ’    # 6c. --scan-nowпјҡз«ӢеҚіжү§иЎҢдёҖж¬Ўжү«жҸҸеҗҺйҖҖеҮәпјҲи°ғиҜ•з”Ёпјү
 138вҶ’    if args.scan_now:
 139вҶ’        logger.info(f"Running immediate scan: type={args.scan_now}")
 140вҶ’        if args.scan_now == "morning":
 141вҶ’            summary = orchestrator.morning_scan()
 142вҶ’        elif args.scan_now == "intraday":
 143вҶ’            summary = orchestrator.intraday_scan()
 144вҶ’        else:
 145вҶ’            summary = orchestrator.eod_check()
 146вҶ’        logger.info(
 147вҶ’            f"Scan complete: buy={summary.buy_count} sell={summary.sell_count} "
 148вҶ’            f"orders={summary.order_count} errors={summary.error_count}"
 149вҶ’        )
 150вҶ’        return
 151вҶ’
 152вҶ’    if args.dry_run:
 153вҶ’        # иҫ“еҮә Phase 5 жЁЎеқ—зҠ¶жҖҒ
 154вҶ’        if components.data_store is not None:
 155вҶ’            logger.info(
 156вҶ’                f"[DryRun] Phase5 modules active: "
 157вҶ’                f"universe={len(components.universe.get_universe())} symbols, "
 158вҶ’                f"signal_valid_bars={config.strategy_matrix.signal_valid_bars}"
 159вҶ’            )
 160вҶ’        else:
 161вҶ’            logger.info("[DryRun] Phase4 fallback mode (local DB not loaded)")
 162вҶ’
 163вҶ’        # Alpaca/IBKR еҗҜеҠЁиҮӘжЈҖ
 164вҶ’        if config.execution.mode in ("semi_auto", "auto"):
 165вҶ’            try:
 166вҶ’                result = components.broker.health_check()
 167вҶ’                if result["status"] == "connected":
 168вҶ’                    logger.info(
 169вҶ’                        f"[DryRun] Broker connected: id={result['account_id']}, "
 170вҶ’                        f"cash=${result['cash']:,.0f}, buying_power=${result['buying_power']:,.0f}, "
 171вҶ’                        f"paper={result['paper']}"
 172вҶ’                    )
 173вҶ’                else:
 174вҶ’                    logger.error(f"[DryRun] Broker health check FAILED: {result}")
 175вҶ’            except AttributeError:
 176вҶ’                logger.info("[DryRun] Broker does not support health_check (PaperBroker)")
 177вҶ’
 178вҶ’        logger.info("Dry-run complete. Exiting.")
 179вҶ’        return
 180вҶ’
 181вҶ’    # 7. еҗҜеҠЁи°ғеәҰеҷЁпјҲжҺҘе…Ҙзңҹе®һеӣһи°ғпјү
 182вҶ’    from mytrader.infra.scheduler import TradingScheduler
 183вҶ’    from mytrader.data.providers.yfinance_provider import YFinanceProvider
 184вҶ’
 185вҶ’    # зӣҳеҗҺж•°жҚ®еўһйҮҸеҗҢжӯҘеӣһи°ғпјҲPhase 5пјү
 186вҶ’    def _on_data_sync() -> None:
 187вҶ’        if components.data_store is None:
 188вҶ’            return
 189вҶ’        from mytrader.data.store import DataSyncService
 190вҶ’        symbols = components.universe.get_universe()
 191вҶ’        logger.info(f"[DataSync] syncing {len(symbols)} symbols...")
 192вҶ’        try:
 193вҶ’            if config.data.provider == "alpaca":
 194вҶ’                from mytrader.data.providers.alpaca_provider import AlpacaDataProvider
 195вҶ’                from datetime import date as _date, timedelta as _td
 196вҶ’                primary = AlpacaDataProvider(
 197вҶ’                    api_key=config.alpaca.api_key,
 198вҶ’                    secret_key=config.alpaca.secret_key,
 199вҶ’                    paper=config.alpaca.paper,
 200вҶ’                )
 201вҶ’                # зӣҳеҗҺеҗҢжӯҘпјҡend з”ЁжҳЁеӨ©йҒҝејҖ SIP е®һж—¶йҷҗеҲ¶
 202вҶ’                end = _date.today() - _td(days=1)
 203вҶ’            else:
 204вҶ’                primary = YFinanceProvider()
 205вҶ’                end = None
 206вҶ’            svc = DataSyncService(
 207вҶ’                store=components.data_store,
 208вҶ’                primary=primary,
 209вҶ’                use_fallback_on_empty=False,
 210вҶ’            )
 211вҶ’            report = svc.sync_all(symbols, max_workers=4, end=end)
 212вҶ’            logger.info(f"[DataSync] done: {report}")
 213вҶ’        except Exception as exc:
 214вҶ’            logger.error(f"[DataSync] failed: {exc}")
 215вҶ’
 216вҶ’    scheduler = TradingScheduler(
 217вҶ’        config=config.scheduler,
 218вҶ’        on_morning_scan=orchestrator.morning_scan,
 219вҶ’        on_intraday_scan=orchestrator.intraday_scan,
 220вҶ’        on_eod_check=orchestrator.eod_check,
 221вҶ’        on_reconciliation=_build_reconciliation_callback(components),
 222вҶ’        on_monthly_reoptimize=lambda: _run_reoptimize(config, logger),
 223вҶ’    )
 224вҶ’
 225вҶ’    # еҗҜеҠЁеүҚе…Ҳжү§иЎҢдёҖж¬Ўж•°жҚ®еҗҢжӯҘпјҲзЎ®дҝқжң¬ең°еә“жңүж•°жҚ®пјү
 226вҶ’    _on_data_sync()
 227вҶ’
 228вҶ’    logger.info("Starting scheduler... (Ctrl+C to stop)")
 229вҶ’    try:
 230вҶ’        scheduler.start()
 231вҶ’    except (KeyboardInterrupt, SystemExit):
 232вҶ’        logger.info("Shutdown signal received")
 233вҶ’    finally:
 234вҶ’        scheduler.shutdown(wait=False)
 235вҶ’        logger.info("MyTrader stopped")
 236вҶ’
 237вҶ’
 238вҶ’def _run_backfill(config: "Any", logger: "Any") -> None:
 239вҶ’    """йҰ–ж¬ЎеӣһеЎ« 5 е№ҙеҺҶеҸІж•°жҚ®гҖӮиҮӘеҠЁеҲ·ж–°жҲҗеҲҶиӮЎеҲ—иЎЁпјҲWikipedia вҶ’ CSVпјүгҖӮ"""
 240вҶ’    from mytrader.data.store import MarketDataStore, DataSyncService
 241вҶ’    from mytrader.data.providers.yfinance_provider import YFinanceProvider
 242вҶ’    from mytrader.universe.manager import UniverseManager
 243вҶ’    from pathlib import Path
 244вҶ’
 245вҶ’    logger.info("[Backfill] initializing MarketDataStore...")
 246вҶ’    store = MarketDataStore()  # дҪҝз”Ёй»ҳи®Өи·Ҝеҫ„ ~/.mytrader/market_data.db
 247вҶ’
 248вҶ’    # иӢҘ universe.csv дёҚеӯҳеңЁжҲ–дёәз©әпјҢд»Һ Wikipedia жӢүеҸ–е®Ңж•ҙжҲҗеҲҶиӮЎеҲ—иЎЁ
 249вҶ’    csv_path = Path("config/universe.csv")
 250вҶ’    need_fetch = (
 251вҶ’        not csv_path.exists()
 252вҶ’        or csv_path.stat().st_size < 100  # еҸӘжңүиЎЁеӨҙжҲ–з©әж–Үд»¶
 253вҶ’    )
 254вҶ’
 255вҶ’    if need_fetch:
 256вҶ’        if csv_path.exists():
 257вҶ’            logger.info(f"[Backfill] universe.csv is empty/corrupt ({csv_path.stat().st_size} bytes), re-fetching...")
 258вҶ’            csv_path.unlink()
 259вҶ’        else:
 260вҶ’            logger.info("[Backfill] universe.csv not found, fetching constituents from Wikipedia...")
 261вҶ’
 262вҶ’        # з”ЁжҢҮе®ҡ CSV и·Ҝеҫ„еҲӣе»ә UniverseManagerпјҢзЎ®дҝқ save_to_csv еҶҷе…ҘжӯЈзЎ®дҪҚзҪ®
 263вҶ’        tmp_universe = UniverseManager(store=store, universe_file=csv_path)
 264вҶ’        tmp_universe.refresh_constituents(save=True)
 265вҶ’
 266вҶ’    universe = UniverseManager(store=store, universe_file=csv_path)
 267вҶ’    symbols = universe.get_universe()
 268вҶ’    logger.info(f"[Backfill] {len(symbols)} symbols to backfill (5 years)")
 269вҶ’
 270вҶ’    if not symbols:
 271вҶ’        logger.error("[Backfill] no symbols to backfill вҖ” abort")
 272вҶ’        return
 273вҶ’
 274вҶ’    from datetime import date as _date, timedelta as _timedelta
 275вҶ’
 276вҶ’    if config.data.provider == "alpaca":
 277вҶ’        from mytrader.data.providers.alpaca_provider import AlpacaDataProvider
 278вҶ’        primary = AlpacaDataProvider(
 279вҶ’            api_key=config.alpaca.api_key,
 280вҶ’            secret_key=config.alpaca.secret_key,
 281вҶ’            paper=config.alpaca.paper,
 282вҶ’        )
 283вҶ’        # Alpaca е…Қиҙ№ SIP дёҚиғҪжҹҘеҪ“ж—Ҙе®һж—¶ж•°жҚ®пјҢend з”ЁжҳЁеӨ©йҒҝејҖйҷҗеҲ¶
 284вҶ’        end = _date.today() - _timedelta(days=1)
 285вҶ’        logger.info(
 286вҶ’            f"[Backfill] using Alpaca provider (end={end}, avoids SIP realtime limit)"
 287вҶ’        )
 288вҶ’    else:
 289вҶ’        primary = YFinanceProvider()
 290вҶ’        end = None
 291вҶ’
 292вҶ’    svc = DataSyncService(store=store, primary=primary, fallback=None,
 293вҶ’                          use_fallback_on_empty=False)
 294вҶ’    report = svc.backfill(symbols, years=5, end=end)
 295вҶ’    logger.info(f"[Backfill] done: {report}")
 296вҶ’
 297вҶ’
 298вҶ’def _run_reoptimize(config: "Any", logger: "Any") -> None:
 299вҶ’    """з«ӢеҚіи§ҰеҸ‘ MatrixBacktest Walk-Forward йҮҚдјҳеҢ–гҖӮ"""
 300вҶ’    from mytrader.data.store import MarketDataStore
 301вҶ’    from mytrader.universe.manager import UniverseManager
 302вҶ’    from mytrader.backtest.matrix_backtest import MatrixBacktest
 303вҶ’    from mytrader.strategy import matrix_runner as _mr_module
 304вҶ’
 305вҶ’    logger.info("[Reoptimize] starting Walk-Forward MatrixBacktest...")
 306вҶ’    store = MarketDataStore()
 307вҶ’    universe = UniverseManager(store=store)
 308вҶ’
 309вҶ’    # йҮҚз®—жіўеҠЁзҺҮеҲҶз»„пјҲзЎ®дҝқеҲҶз»„жҳҜжңҖж–°зҡ„пјү
 310вҶ’    universe.recompute_volatility_tiers(max_workers=4)
 311вҶ’
 312вҶ’    mb = MatrixBacktest(store=store, universe=universe, years=5, top_k=2)
 313вҶ’    strategies = ["dual_ma", "rsi", "macd", "bollinger"]
 314вҶ’    param_grids = {
 315вҶ’        "dual_ma": {"fast": [5, 10], "slow": [20, 40, 60]},
 316вҶ’        "rsi":     {"period": [14], "oversold": [30], "overbought": [70]},
 317вҶ’        "macd":    {"fast": [12], "slow": [26], "signal_period": [9]},
 318вҶ’        "bollinger": {"period": [20], "std_dev": [2.0]},
 319вҶ’    }
 320вҶ’
 321вҶ’    output = Path("config/strategy_weights.json")
 322вҶ’    report = mb.run(strategies=strategies, param_grids=param_grids, output_file=output)
 323вҶ’    logger.info(
 324вҶ’        f"[Reoptimize] done: {len(report.groups)} groups, "
 325вҶ’        f"output={output}"
 326вҶ’    )
 327вҶ’
 328вҶ’    # зғӯеҠ иҪҪпјҲеҰӮжһң StrategyMatrixRunner е·ІеңЁиҝҗиЎҢпјү
 329вҶ’    try:
 330вҶ’        from mytrader.strategy.matrix_runner import StrategyMatrixRunner
 331вҶ’        logger.info("[Reoptimize] weights reloaded into StrategyMatrixRunner")
 332вҶ’    except Exception:
 333вҶ’        pass
 334вҶ’
 335вҶ’
 336вҶ’def _build_reconciliation_callback(components: "Any") -> "Callable":
 337вҶ’    """жһ„е»әеҜ№иҙҰеӣһи°ғпјҲзӣҳеҗҺ 16:30 ETпјүгҖӮ"""
 338вҶ’    from loguru import logger
 339вҶ’
 340вҶ’    def on_reconciliation() -> None:
 341вҶ’        try:
 342вҶ’            from mytrader.portfolio.reconciliation import ReconciliationService
 343вҶ’            svc = ReconciliationService(
 344вҶ’                tracker=components.tracker,
 345вҶ’                broker=components.broker,
 346вҶ’                event_bus=components.bus,
 347вҶ’                auto_sync=False,
 348вҶ’            )
 349вҶ’            report = svc.reconcile()
 350вҶ’            if report.has_diff:
 351вҶ’                logger.warning(
 352вҶ’                    f"[Reconciliation] {len(report.diffs)} diff(s) found: "
 353вҶ’                    f"{[d.symbol for d in report.diffs]}"
 354вҶ’                )
 355вҶ’            else:
 356вҶ’                logger.info("[Reconciliation] No diffs вҖ” positions match")
 357вҶ’
 358вҶ’            # ж— и®әжңүж— е·®ејӮйғҪжҺЁйҖҒеҜ№иҙҰжҠҘе‘Ҡ
 359вҶ’            if components.notification:
 360вҶ’                try:
 361вҶ’                    from datetime import datetime, timezone
 362вҶ’                    ts = datetime.now(timezone.utc).strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S UTC")
 363вҶ’                    if report.has_diff:
 364вҶ’                        diff_syms = [d.symbol for d in report.diffs]
 365вҶ’                        text = (
 366вҶ’                            "вҡ пёҸ *жҢҒд»“еҜ№иҙҰжҠҘе‘Ҡ*\n"
 367вҶ’                            f"ж—¶й—ҙпјҡ{ts}\n"
 368вҶ’                            f"еҸ‘зҺ° {len(report.diffs)} дёӘж Үзҡ„жҢҒд»“е·®ејӮпјҡ\n"
 369вҶ’                            f"{', '.join(diff_syms[:10])}"
 370вҶ’                            + (f" зӯү{len(diff_syms)}еҸӘ" if len(diff_syms) > 10 else "")
 371вҶ’                            + "\nиҜ·жЈҖжҹҘ broker дёҺжң¬ең°и®°еҪ•"
 372вҶ’                        )
 373вҶ’                    else:
 374вҶ’                        text = (
 375вҶ’                            "вң… *жҢҒд»“еҜ№иҙҰжҠҘе‘Ҡ*\n"
 376вҶ’                            f"ж—¶й—ҙпјҡ{ts}\n"
 377вҶ’                            "жҢҒд»“дёҖиҮҙпјҢж— е·®ејӮ"
 378вҶ’                        )
 379вҶ’                    components.notification.send_message(text)
 380вҶ’                except Exception as exc:
 381вҶ’                    logger.warning(f"[Reconciliation] notification failed: {exc}")
 382вҶ’        except Exception as exc:
 383вҶ’            logger.error(f"[Reconciliation] Failed: {exc}")
 384вҶ’
 385вҶ’    return on_reconciliation
 386вҶ’
 387вҶ’
 388вҶ’if __name__ == "__main__":
 389вҶ’    main()
 390вҶ’
 391вҶ’   1вҶ’"""MyTrader зі»з»ҹеҗҜеҠЁе…ҘеҸЈгҖӮ
   2вҶ’
   3вҶ’з”Ёжі•пјҡ
   4вҶ’    python main.py                        # paper жЁЎејҸпјҢй»ҳи®Өй…ҚзҪ®
   5вҶ’    python main.py --mode semi_auto       # еҚҠиҮӘеҠЁпјҲжҺЁйҖҒйҖҡзҹҘпјҢдәәе·ҘзЎ®и®Өпјү
   6вҶ’    python main.py --mode auto            # е…ЁиҮӘеҠЁпјҲзӣҙжҺҘдёӢеҚ•пјү
   7вҶ’    python main.py --config path/to.yaml  # иҮӘе®ҡд№үй…ҚзҪ®ж–Үд»¶
   8вҶ’    python main.py --dry-run              # д»…жЈҖжҹҘй…ҚзҪ®е’Ңдҫқиө–пјҢдёҚеҗҜеҠЁи°ғеәҰеҷЁ
   9вҶ’    python main.py --scan-now morning     # з«ӢеҚіжү§иЎҢдёҖж¬ЎзӣҳеүҚжү«жҸҸпјҲи°ғиҜ•з”Ёпјү
  10вҶ’    python main.py --reoptimize           # з«ӢеҚіи§ҰеҸ‘ MatrixBacktestпјҲWalk-Forward йҮҚдјҳеҢ–пјү
  11вҶ’    python main.py --backfill             # йҰ–ж¬ЎеӣһеЎ« 5 е№ҙеҺҶеҸІж•°жҚ®пјҲMarketDataStoreпјү
  12вҶ’
  13вҶ’зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸиҰҶзӣ–пјҲйҖҡиҝҮ .env ж–Үд»¶пјүпјҡ
  14вҶ’    EXECUTION__MODE=semi_auto
  15вҶ’    ALPACA__API_KEY=your_key
  16вҶ’    NOTIFICATION__TELEGRAM_ENABLED=true
  17вҶ’    WATCHLIST__SYMBOLS='["AAPL","TSLA"]'
  18вҶ’"""
  19вҶ’
  20вҶ’from __future__ import annotations
  21вҶ’
  22вҶ’import argparse
  23вҶ’import sys
  24вҶ’from pathlib import Path
  25вҶ’
  26вҶ’
  27вҶ’def parse_args() -> argparse.Namespace:
  28вҶ’    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(
  29вҶ’        prog="mytrader",
  30вҶ’        description="MyTrader вҖ” иҪ»йҮҸзә§ж—ҘеҶ…/зҹӯзәҝдәӨжҳ“зі»з»ҹ",
  31вҶ’    )
  32вҶ’    parser.add_argument(
  33вҶ’        "--mode",
  34вҶ’        choices=["paper", "semi_auto", "auto"],
  35вҶ’        default=None,
  36вҶ’        help="жү§иЎҢжЁЎејҸпјҲиҰҶзӣ–й…ҚзҪ®ж–Үд»¶пјү: paper | semi_auto | auto",
  37вҶ’    )
  38вҶ’    parser.add_argument(
  39вҶ’        "--config",
  40вҶ’        type=str,
  41вҶ’        default=None,
  42вҶ’        metavar="PATH",
  43вҶ’        help="YAML й…ҚзҪ®ж–Үд»¶и·Ҝеҫ„пјҲй»ҳи®ӨиҮӘеҠЁжҹҘжүҫ config/default.yamlпјү",
  44вҶ’    )
  45вҶ’    parser.add_argument(
  46вҶ’        "--log-dir",
  47вҶ’        type=str,
  48вҶ’        default="logs",
  49вҶ’        metavar="DIR",
  50вҶ’        help="ж—Ҙеҝ—зӣ®еҪ•пјҲй»ҳи®Ө logs/пјү",
  51вҶ’    )
  52вҶ’    parser.add_argument(
  53вҶ’        "--dry-run",
  54вҶ’        action="store_true",
  55вҶ’        help="д»…еҲқе§ӢеҢ–е№¶жЈҖжҹҘй…ҚзҪ®пјҢдёҚеҗҜеҠЁи°ғеәҰеҷЁ",
  56вҶ’    )
  57вҶ’    parser.add_argument(
  58вҶ’        "--db",
  59вҶ’        type=str,
  60вҶ’        default="mytrader.db",
  61вҶ’        metavar="PATH",
  62вҶ’        help="SQLite ж•°жҚ®еә“и·Ҝеҫ„пјҲй»ҳи®Ө mytrader.dbпјү",
  63вҶ’    )
  64вҶ’    parser.add_argument(
  65вҶ’        "--scan-now",
  66вҶ’        choices=["morning", "intraday", "eod"],
  67вҶ’        default=None,
  68вҶ’        metavar="TYPE",
  69вҶ’        help="з«ӢеҚіжү§иЎҢдёҖж¬ЎжҢҮе®ҡзұ»еһӢзҡ„жү«жҸҸпјҢдёҚеҗҜеҠЁи°ғеәҰеҷЁпјҲи°ғиҜ•з”Ёпјү",
  70вҶ’    )
  71вҶ’    parser.add_argument(
  72вҶ’        "--reoptimize",
  73вҶ’        action="store_true",
  74вҶ’        help="з«ӢеҚіи§ҰеҸ‘ MatrixBacktest Walk-Forward йҮҚдјҳеҢ–пјҢжӣҙж–° strategy_weights.json",
  75вҶ’    )
  76вҶ’    parser.add_argument(
  77вҶ’        "--backfill",
  78вҶ’        action="store_true",
  79вҶ’        help="йҰ–ж¬ЎеӣһеЎ« 5 е№ҙеҺҶеҸІж•°жҚ®еҲ° MarketDataStoreпјҲдёҖж¬ЎжҖ§ж“ҚдҪңпјү",
  80вҶ’    )
  81вҶ’    return parser.parse_args()
  82вҶ’
  83вҶ’
  84вҶ’def main() -> None:
  85вҶ’    args = parse_args()
  86вҶ’
  87вҶ’    # 1. еҲқе§ӢеҢ–ж—Ҙеҝ—пјҲжңҖе…Ҳжү§иЎҢпјү
  88вҶ’    from mytrader.monitor.logger_setup import setup_logger
  89вҶ’    setup_logger(log_dir=args.log_dir, level="INFO")
  90вҶ’
  91вҶ’    from loguru import logger
  92вҶ’    logger.info(f"MyTrader starting: mode={args.mode or 'from_config'} dry_run={args.dry_run}")
  93вҶ’
  94вҶ’    # 2. еҠ иҪҪй…ҚзҪ®
  95вҶ’    from mytrader.infra.config import load_config
  96вҶ’    config = load_config(args.config)
  97вҶ’
  98вҶ’    # CLI --mode иҰҶзӣ–й…ҚзҪ®ж–Үд»¶
  99вҶ’    if args.mode is not None:
 100вҶ’        object.__setattr__(config.execution, "mode", args.mode)
 101вҶ’        logger.info(f"Execution mode overridden by CLI: {args.mode}")
 102вҶ’
 103вҶ’    logger.info(
 104вҶ’        f"Config loaded: mode={config.execution.mode} broker={config.execution.broker} "
 105вҶ’        f"scheduler.enabled={config.scheduler.enabled} "
 106вҶ’        f"watchlist={config.watchlist.symbols}"
 107вҶ’    )
 108вҶ’
 109вҶ’    # 3. иЈ…й…Қдҫқиө–
 110вҶ’    from mytrader.infra.container import Container
 111вҶ’    components = Container.build(config, db_url=f"sqlite:///{args.db}")
 112вҶ’
 113вҶ’    # 4. еҒҘеә·жЈҖжҹҘ
 114вҶ’    report = components.health.run_all()
 115вҶ’    logger.info(f"Health check: {report.status} ({report.checks})")
 116вҶ’    if not report.is_healthy:
 117вҶ’        for name in report.failed_checks:
 118вҶ’            logger.warning(f"Health check FAILED: {name} вҖ” {report.details.get(name)}")
 119вҶ’
 120вҶ’    # 5. жһ„е»әжү«жҸҸзј–жҺ’еҷЁ
 121вҶ’    from mytrader.scan_orchestrator import build_orchestrator
 122вҶ’    orchestrator = build_orchestrator(components)
 123вҶ’
 124вҶ’    mode_label = "Phase 5 (multi-strategy matrix)" if orchestrator._use_phase5 else "Phase 4 (single-strategy)"
 125вҶ’    logger.info(f"[Orchestrator] Built in {mode_label} mode")
 126вҶ’
 127вҶ’    # 6a. --backfillпјҡйҰ–ж¬ЎеӣһеЎ«еҺҶеҸІж•°жҚ®
 128вҶ’    if args.backfill:
 129вҶ’        _run_backfill(config, logger)
 130вҶ’        return
 131вҶ’
 132вҶ’    # 6b. --reoptimizeпјҡз«ӢеҚіи§ҰеҸ‘ MatrixBacktest
 133вҶ’    if args.reoptimize:
 134вҶ’        _run_reoptimize(config, logger)
 135вҶ’        return
 136вҶ’
 137вҶ’    # 6c. --scan-nowпјҡз«ӢеҚіжү§иЎҢдёҖж¬Ўжү«жҸҸеҗҺйҖҖеҮәпјҲи°ғиҜ•з”Ёпјү
 138вҶ’    if args.scan_now:
 139вҶ’        logger.info(f"Running immediate scan: type={args.scan_now}")
 140вҶ’        if args.scan_now == "morning":
 141вҶ’            summary = orchestrator.morning_scan()
 142вҶ’        elif args.scan_now == "intraday":
 143вҶ’            summary = orchestrator.intraday_scan()
 144вҶ’        else:
 145вҶ’            summary = orchestrator.eod_check()
 146вҶ’        logger.info(
 147вҶ’            f"Scan complete: buy={summary.buy_count} sell={summary.sell_count} "
 148вҶ’            f"orders={summary.order_count} errors={summary.error_count}"
 149вҶ’        )
 150вҶ’        return
 151вҶ’
 152вҶ’    if args.dry_run:
 153вҶ’        # иҫ“еҮә Phase 5 жЁЎеқ—зҠ¶жҖҒ
 154вҶ’        if components.data_store is not None:
 155вҶ’            logger.info(
 156вҶ’                f"[DryRun] Phase5 modules active: "
 157вҶ’                f"universe={len(components.universe.get_universe())} symbols, "
 158вҶ’                f"signal_valid_bars={config.strategy_matrix.signal_valid_bars}"
 159вҶ’            )
 160вҶ’        else:
 161вҶ’            logger.info("[DryRun] Phase4 fallback mode (local DB not loaded)")
 162вҶ’
 163вҶ’        # Alpaca/IBKR еҗҜеҠЁиҮӘжЈҖ
 164вҶ’        if config.execution.mode in ("semi_auto", "auto"):
 165вҶ’            try:
 166вҶ’                result = components.broker.health_check()
 167вҶ’                if result["status"] == "connected":
 168вҶ’                    logger.info(
 169вҶ’                        f"[DryRun] Broker connected: id={result['account_id']}, "
 170вҶ’                        f"cash=${result['cash']:,.0f}, buying_power=${result['buying_power']:,.0f}, "
 171вҶ’                        f"paper={result['paper']}"
 172вҶ’                    )
 173вҶ’                else:
 174вҶ’                    logger.error(f"[DryRun] Broker health check FAILED: {result}")
 175вҶ’            except AttributeError:
 176вҶ’                logger.info("[DryRun] Broker does not support health_check (PaperBroker)")
 177вҶ’
 178вҶ’        logger.info("Dry-run complete. Exiting.")
 179вҶ’        return
 180вҶ’
 181вҶ’    # 7. еҗҜеҠЁи°ғеәҰеҷЁпјҲжҺҘе…Ҙзңҹе®һеӣһи°ғпјү
 182вҶ’    from mytrader.infra.scheduler import TradingScheduler
 183вҶ’    from mytrader.data.providers.yfinance_provider import YFinanceProvider
 184вҶ’
 185вҶ’    # зӣҳеҗҺж•°жҚ®еўһйҮҸеҗҢжӯҘеӣһи°ғпјҲPhase 5пјү
 186вҶ’    def _on_data_sync() -> None:
 187вҶ’        if components.data_store is None:
 188вҶ’            return
 189вҶ’        from mytrader.data.store import DataSyncService
 190вҶ’        symbols = components.universe.get_universe()
 191вҶ’        logger.info(f"[DataSync] syncing {len(symbols)} symbols...")
 192вҶ’        try:
 193вҶ’            if config.data.provider == "alpaca":
 194вҶ’                from mytrader.data.providers.alpaca_provider import AlpacaDataProvider
 195вҶ’                from datetime import date as _date, timedelta as _td
 196вҶ’                primary = AlpacaDataProvider(
 197вҶ’                    api_key=config.alpaca.api_key,
 198вҶ’                    secret_key=config.alpaca.secret_key,
 199вҶ’                    paper=config.alpaca.paper,
 200вҶ’                )
 201вҶ’                # зӣҳеҗҺеҗҢжӯҘпјҡend з”ЁжҳЁеӨ©йҒҝејҖ SIP е®һж—¶йҷҗеҲ¶
 202вҶ’                end = _date.today() - _td(days=1)
 203вҶ’            else:
 204вҶ’                primary = YFinanceProvider()
 205вҶ’                end = None
 206вҶ’            svc = DataSyncService(
 207вҶ’                store=components.data_store,
 208вҶ’                primary=primary,
 209вҶ’                use_fallback_on_empty=False,
 210вҶ’            )
 211вҶ’            report = svc.sync_all(symbols, max_workers=4, end=end)
 212вҶ’            logger.info(f"[DataSync] done: {report}")
 213вҶ’        except Exception as exc:
 214вҶ’            logger.error(f"[DataSync] failed: {exc}")
 215вҶ’
 216вҶ’    scheduler = TradingScheduler(
 217вҶ’        config=config.scheduler,
 218вҶ’        on_morning_scan=orchestrator.morning_scan,
 219вҶ’        on_intraday_scan=orchestrator.intraday_scan,
 220вҶ’        on_eod_check=orchestrator.eod_check,
 221вҶ’        on_reconciliation=_build_reconciliation_callback(components),
 222вҶ’        on_monthly_reoptimize=lambda: _run_reoptimize(config, logger),
 223вҶ’    )
 224вҶ’
 225вҶ’    # еҗҜеҠЁеүҚе…Ҳжү§иЎҢдёҖж¬Ўж•°жҚ®еҗҢжӯҘпјҲзЎ®дҝқжң¬ең°еә“жңүж•°жҚ®пјү
 226вҶ’    _on_data_sync()
 227вҶ’
 228вҶ’    logger.info("Starting scheduler... (Ctrl+C to stop)")
 229вҶ’    try:
 230вҶ’        scheduler.start()
 231вҶ’    except (KeyboardInterrupt, SystemExit):
 232вҶ’        logger.info("Shutdown signal received")
 233вҶ’    finally:
 234вҶ’        scheduler.shutdown(wait=False)
 235вҶ’        logger.info("MyTrader stopped")
 236вҶ’
 237вҶ’
 238вҶ’def _run_backfill(config: "Any", logger: "Any") -> None:
 239вҶ’    """йҰ–ж¬ЎеӣһеЎ« 5 е№ҙеҺҶеҸІж•°жҚ®гҖӮиҮӘеҠЁеҲ·ж–°жҲҗеҲҶиӮЎеҲ—иЎЁпјҲWikipedia вҶ’ CSVпјүгҖӮ"""
 240вҶ’    from mytrader.data.store import MarketDataStore, DataSyncService
 241вҶ’    from mytrader.data.providers.yfinance_provider import YFinanceProvider
 242вҶ’    from mytrader.universe.manager import UniverseManager
 243вҶ’    from pathlib import Path
 244вҶ’
 245вҶ’    logger.info("[Backfill] initializing MarketDataStore...")
 246вҶ’    store = MarketDataStore()  # дҪҝз”Ёй»ҳи®Өи·Ҝеҫ„ ~/.mytrader/market_data.db
 247вҶ’
 248вҶ’    # иӢҘ universe.csv дёҚеӯҳеңЁжҲ–дёәз©әпјҢд»Һ Wikipedia жӢүеҸ–е®Ңж•ҙжҲҗеҲҶиӮЎеҲ—иЎЁ
 249вҶ’    csv_path = Path("config/universe.csv")
 250вҶ’    need_fetch = (
 251вҶ’        not csv_path.exists()
 252вҶ’        or csv_path.stat().st_size < 100  # еҸӘжңүиЎЁеӨҙжҲ–з©әж–Үд»¶
 253вҶ’    )
 254вҶ’
 255вҶ’    if need_fetch:
 256вҶ’        if csv_path.exists():
 257вҶ’            logger.info(f"[Backfill] universe.csv is empty/corrupt ({csv_path.stat().st_size} bytes), re-fetching...")
 258вҶ’            csv_path.unlink()
 259вҶ’        else:
 260вҶ’            logger.info("[Backfill] universe.csv not found, fetching constituents from Wikipedia...")
 261вҶ’
 262вҶ’        # з”ЁжҢҮе®ҡ CSV и·Ҝеҫ„еҲӣе»ә UniverseManagerпјҢзЎ®дҝқ save_to_csv еҶҷе…ҘжӯЈзЎ®дҪҚзҪ®
 263вҶ’        tmp_universe = UniverseManager(store=store, universe_file=csv_path)
 264вҶ’        tmp_universe.refresh_constituents(save=True)
 265вҶ’
 266вҶ’    universe = UniverseManager(store=store, universe_file=csv_path)
 267вҶ’    symbols = universe.get_universe()
 268вҶ’    logger.info(f"[Backfill] {len(symbols)} symbols to backfill (5 years)")
 269вҶ’
 270вҶ’    if not symbols:
 271вҶ’        logger.error("[Backfill] no symbols to backfill вҖ” abort")
 272вҶ’        return
 273вҶ’
 274вҶ’    from datetime import date as _date, timedelta as _timedelta
 275вҶ’
 276вҶ’    if config.data.provider == "alpaca":
 277вҶ’        from mytrader.data.providers.alpaca_provider import AlpacaDataProvider
 278вҶ’        primary = AlpacaDataProvider(
 279вҶ’            api_key=config.alpaca.api_key,
 280вҶ’            secret_key=config.alpaca.secret_key,
 281вҶ’            paper=config.alpaca.paper,
 282вҶ’        )
 283вҶ’        # Alpaca е…Қиҙ№ SIP дёҚиғҪжҹҘеҪ“ж—Ҙе®һж—¶ж•°жҚ®пјҢend з”ЁжҳЁеӨ©йҒҝејҖйҷҗеҲ¶
 284вҶ’        end = _date.today() - _timedelta(days=1)
 285вҶ’        logger.info(
 286вҶ’            f"[Backfill] using Alpaca provider (end={end}, avoids SIP realtime limit)"
 287вҶ’        )
 288вҶ’    else:
 289вҶ’        primary = YFinanceProvider()
 290вҶ’        end = None
 291вҶ’
 292вҶ’    svc = DataSyncService(store=store, primary=primary, fallback=None,
 293вҶ’                          use_fallback_on_empty=False)
 294вҶ’    report = svc.backfill(symbols, years=5, end=end)
 295вҶ’    logger.info(f"[Backfill] done: {report}")
 296вҶ’
 297вҶ’
 298вҶ’def _run_reoptimize(config: "Any", logger: "Any") -> None:
 299вҶ’    """з«ӢеҚіи§ҰеҸ‘ MatrixBacktest Walk-Forward йҮҚдјҳеҢ–гҖӮ"""
 300вҶ’    from mytrader.data.store import MarketDataStore
 301вҶ’    from mytrader.universe.manager import UniverseManager
 302вҶ’    from mytrader.backtest.matrix_backtest import MatrixBacktest
 303вҶ’    from mytrader.strategy import matrix_runner as _mr_module
 304вҶ’
 305вҶ’    logger.info("[Reoptimize] starting Walk-Forward MatrixBacktest...")
 306вҶ’    store = MarketDataStore()
 307вҶ’    universe = UniverseManager(store=store)
 308вҶ’
 309вҶ’    # йҮҚз®—жіўеҠЁзҺҮеҲҶз»„пјҲзЎ®дҝқеҲҶз»„жҳҜжңҖж–°зҡ„пјү
 310вҶ’    universe.recompute_volatility_tiers(max_workers=4)
 311вҶ’
 312вҶ’    mb = MatrixBacktest(store=store, universe=universe, years=5, top_k=2)
 313вҶ’    strategies = ["dual_ma", "rsi", "macd", "bollinger"]
 314вҶ’    param_grids = {
 315вҶ’        "dual_ma": {"fast": [5, 10], "slow": [20, 40, 60]},
 316вҶ’        "rsi":     {"period": [14], "oversold": [30], "overbought": [70]},
 317вҶ’        "macd":    {"fast": [12], "slow": [26], "signal_period": [9]},
 318вҶ’        "bollinger": {"period": [20], "std_dev": [2.0]},
 319вҶ’    }
 320вҶ’
 321вҶ’    output = Path("config/strategy_weights.json")
 322вҶ’    report = mb.run(strategies=strategies, param_grids=param_grids, output_file=output)
 323вҶ’    logger.info(
 324вҶ’        f"[Reoptimize] done: {len(report.groups)} groups, "
 325вҶ’        f"output={output}"
 326вҶ’    )
 327вҶ’
 328вҶ’    # зғӯеҠ иҪҪпјҲеҰӮжһң StrategyMatrixRunner е·ІеңЁиҝҗиЎҢпјү
 329вҶ’    try:
 330вҶ’        from mytrader.strategy.matrix_runner import StrategyMatrixRunner
 331вҶ’        logger.info("[Reoptimize] weights reloaded into StrategyMatrixRunner")
 332вҶ’    except Exception:
 333вҶ’        pass
 334вҶ’
 335вҶ’
 336вҶ’def _build_reconciliation_callback(components: "Any") -> "Callable":
 337вҶ’    """жһ„е»әеҜ№иҙҰеӣһи°ғпјҲзӣҳеҗҺ 16:30 ETпјүгҖӮ"""
 338вҶ’    from loguru import logger
 339вҶ’
 340вҶ’    def on_reconciliation() -> None:
 341вҶ’        try:
 342вҶ’            from mytrader.portfolio.reconciliation import ReconciliationService
 343вҶ’            svc = ReconciliationService(
 344вҶ’                tracker=components.tracker,
 345вҶ’                broker=components.broker,
 346вҶ’                event_bus=components.bus,
 347вҶ’                auto_sync=False,
 348вҶ’            )
 349вҶ’            report = svc.reconcile()
 350вҶ’            if report.has_diff:
 351вҶ’                logger.warning(
 352вҶ’                    f"[Reconciliation] {len(report.diffs)} diff(s) found: "
 353вҶ’                    f"{[d.symbol for d in report.diffs]}"
 354вҶ’                )
 355вҶ’            else:
 356вҶ’                logger.info("[Reconciliation] No diffs вҖ” positions match")
 357вҶ’
 358вҶ’            # ж— и®әжңүж— е·®ејӮйғҪжҺЁйҖҒеҜ№иҙҰжҠҘе‘Ҡ
 359вҶ’            if components.notification:
 360вҶ’                try:
 361вҶ’                    from datetime import datetime, timezone
 362вҶ’                    ts = datetime.now(timezone.utc).strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S UTC")
 363вҶ’                    if report.has_diff:
 364вҶ’                        diff_syms = [d.symbol for d in report.diffs]
 365вҶ’                        text = (
 366вҶ’                            "вҡ пёҸ *жҢҒд»“еҜ№иҙҰжҠҘе‘Ҡ*\n"
 367вҶ’                            f"ж—¶й—ҙпјҡ{ts}\n"
 368вҶ’                            f"еҸ‘зҺ° {len(report.diffs)} дёӘж Үзҡ„жҢҒд»“е·®ејӮпјҡ\n"
 369вҶ’                            f"{', '.join(diff_syms[:10])}"
 370вҶ’                            + (f" зӯү{len(diff_syms)}еҸӘ" if len(diff_syms) > 10 else "")
 371вҶ’                            + "\nиҜ·жЈҖжҹҘ broker дёҺжң¬ең°и®°еҪ•"
 372вҶ’                        )
 373вҶ’                    else:
 374вҶ’                        text = (
 375вҶ’                            "вң… *жҢҒд»“еҜ№иҙҰжҠҘе‘Ҡ*\n"
 376вҶ’                            f"ж—¶й—ҙпјҡ{ts}\n"
 377вҶ’                            "жҢҒд»“дёҖиҮҙпјҢж— е·®ејӮ"
 378вҶ’                        )
 379вҶ’                    components.notification.send_message(text)
 380вҶ’                except Exception as exc:
 381вҶ’                    logger.warning(f"[Reconciliation] notification failed: {exc}")
 382вҶ’        except Exception as exc:
 383вҶ’            logger.error(f"[Reconciliation] Failed: {exc}")
 384вҶ’
 385вҶ’    return on_reconciliation
 386вҶ’
 387вҶ’
 388вҶ’if __name__ == "__main__":
 389вҶ’    main()
 390вҶ’
 391вҶ’   1вҶ’"""еҸҢеқҮзәҝдәӨеҸүзӯ–з•ҘпјҲDual MA CrossoverпјүгҖӮ
   2вҶ’
   3вҶ’дҝЎеҸ·и§„еҲҷпјҡ
   4вҶ’    - зҹӯжңҹеқҮзәҝдёҠз©ҝй•ҝжңҹеқҮзәҝ вҶ’ BUY  (+1)
   5вҶ’    - зҹӯжңҹеқҮзәҝдёӢз©ҝй•ҝжңҹеқҮзәҝ вҶ’ SELL (-1)
   6вҶ’    - еҗҰеҲҷ               вҶ’ HOLD  (0)
   7вҶ’
   8вҶ’жіЁж„ҸпјҡдҝЎеҸ·ејәеҲ¶ shift(1)пјҢдҪҝз”ЁеүҚдёҖж № K зәҝзҡ„еқҮзәҝзҠ¶жҖҒеҒҡеҶізӯ–пјҢ
   9вҶ’      йҒҝе…ҚеүҚи§ҶеҒҸе·®пјҲдёҚдҪҝз”ЁеҪ“еӨ©ж”¶зӣҳд»·пјүгҖӮ
  10вҶ’"""
  11вҶ’
  12вҶ’from __future__ import annotations
  13вҶ’
  14вҶ’import pandas as pd
  15вҶ’
  16вҶ’from mytrader.strategy.indicators import sma, crossed_above, crossed_below
  17вҶ’from mytrader.strategy.registry import register_strategy
  18вҶ’
  19вҶ’
  20вҶ’@register_strategy("dual_ma")
  21вҶ’def dual_ma_signal(
  22вҶ’    close: pd.Series,
  23вҶ’    fast: int = 10,
  24вҶ’    slow: int = 30,
  25вҶ’) -> pd.Series:
  26вҶ’    """еҸҢеқҮзәҝдәӨеҸүдҝЎеҸ·гҖӮ
  27вҶ’
  28вҶ’    Args:
  29вҶ’        close: ж”¶зӣҳд»· Series
  30вҶ’        fast:  зҹӯжңҹеқҮзәҝе‘ЁжңҹпјҲй»ҳи®Ө 10пјү
  31вҶ’        slow:  й•ҝжңҹеқҮзәҝе‘ЁжңҹпјҲй»ҳи®Ө 30пјү
  32вҶ’
  33вҶ’    Returns:
  34вҶ’        дҝЎеҸ· Seriesпјҡ1=BUY, -1=SELL, 0=HOLDпјҢдёҺ close еҗҢзҙўеј•
  35вҶ’    """
  36вҶ’    fast_ma = sma(close, fast)
  37вҶ’    slow_ma = sma(close, slow)
  38вҶ’
  39вҶ’    buy_signal  = crossed_above(fast_ma, slow_ma).astype(int)
  40вҶ’    sell_signal = crossed_below(fast_ma, slow_ma).astype(int)
  41вҶ’
  42вҶ’    signal = buy_signal - sell_signal  # 1, -1, 0
  43вҶ’
  44вҶ’    # вҡ пёҸ е…ій”®пјҡshift(1) йҒҝе…ҚеүҚи§ҶеҒҸе·®
  45вҶ’    # дҪҝз”ЁеүҚдёҖж № K зәҝзЎ®и®Өзҡ„еқҮзәҝзҠ¶жҖҒпјҢеңЁеҪ“еүҚ K зәҝејҖзӣҳж—¶жү§иЎҢ
  46вҶ’    return signal.shift(1).fillna(0).astype(int)
  47вҶ’   1вҶ’"""еҸҢеқҮзәҝдәӨеҸүзӯ–з•ҘпјҲDual MA CrossoverпјүгҖӮ
   2вҶ’
   3вҶ’дҝЎеҸ·и§„еҲҷпјҡ
   4вҶ’    - зҹӯжңҹеқҮзәҝдёҠз©ҝй•ҝжңҹеқҮзәҝ вҶ’ BUY  (+1)
   5вҶ’    - зҹӯжңҹеқҮзәҝдёӢз©ҝй•ҝжңҹеқҮзәҝ вҶ’ SELL (-1)
   6вҶ’    - еҗҰеҲҷ               вҶ’ HOLD  (0)
   7вҶ’
   8вҶ’жіЁж„ҸпјҡдҝЎеҸ·ејәеҲ¶ shift(1)пјҢдҪҝз”ЁеүҚдёҖж № K зәҝзҡ„еқҮзәҝзҠ¶жҖҒеҒҡеҶізӯ–пјҢ
   9вҶ’      йҒҝе…ҚеүҚи§ҶеҒҸе·®пјҲдёҚдҪҝз”ЁеҪ“еӨ©ж”¶зӣҳд»·пјүгҖӮ
  10вҶ’"""
  11вҶ’
  12вҶ’from __future__ import annotations
  13вҶ’
  14вҶ’import pandas as pd
  15вҶ’
  16вҶ’from mytrader.strategy.indicators import sma, crossed_above, crossed_below
  17вҶ’from mytrader.strategy.registry import register_strategy
  18вҶ’
  19вҶ’
  20вҶ’@register_strategy("dual_ma")
  21вҶ’def dual_ma_signal(
  22вҶ’    close: pd.Series,
  23вҶ’    fast: int = 10,
  24вҶ’    slow: int = 30,
  25вҶ’) -> pd.Series:
  26вҶ’    """еҸҢеқҮзәҝдәӨеҸүдҝЎеҸ·гҖӮ
  27вҶ’
  28вҶ’    Args:
  29вҶ’        close: ж”¶зӣҳд»· Series
  30вҶ’        fast:  зҹӯжңҹеқҮзәҝе‘ЁжңҹпјҲй»ҳи®Ө 10пјү
  31вҶ’        slow:  й•ҝжңҹеқҮзәҝе‘ЁжңҹпјҲй»ҳи®Ө 30пјү
  32вҶ’
  33вҶ’    Returns:
  34вҶ’        дҝЎеҸ· Seriesпјҡ1=BUY, -1=SELL, 0=HOLDпјҢдёҺ close еҗҢзҙўеј•
  35вҶ’    """
  36вҶ’    fast_ma = sma(close, fast)
  37вҶ’    slow_ma = sma(close, slow)
  38вҶ’
  39вҶ’    buy_signal  = crossed_above(fast_ma, slow_ma).astype(int)
  40вҶ’    sell_signal = crossed_below(fast_ma, slow_ma).astype(int)
  41вҶ’
  42вҶ’    signal = buy_signal - sell_signal  # 1, -1, 0
  43вҶ’
  44вҶ’    # вҡ пёҸ е…ій”®пјҡshift(1) йҒҝе…ҚеүҚи§ҶеҒҸе·®
  45вҶ’    # дҪҝз”ЁеүҚдёҖж № K зәҝзЎ®и®Өзҡ„еқҮзәҝзҠ¶жҖҒпјҢеңЁеҪ“еүҚ K зәҝејҖзӣҳж—¶жү§иЎҢ
  46вҶ’    return signal.shift(1).fillna(0).astype(int)
  47вҶ’   1вҶ’"""RSI еқҮеҖјеӣһеҪ’зӯ–з•ҘгҖӮ
   2вҶ’
   3вҶ’дҝЎеҸ·и§„еҲҷпјҡ
   4вҶ’    - RSI < oversoldпјҲй»ҳи®Ө 30пјүвҶ’ и¶…еҚ–пјҢBUY  (+1)
   5вҶ’    - RSI > overboughtпјҲй»ҳи®Ө 70пјүвҶ’ и¶…д№°пјҢSELL (-1)
   6вҶ’    - еҗҰеҲҷ                      вҶ’ HOLD  (0)
   7вҶ’
   8вҶ’йҖӮз”ЁеңәжҷҜпјҡйңҮиҚЎеёӮпјӣеҚ•иҫ№и¶ӢеҠҝдёӯдјҡйў‘з№ҒйҖҶеҠҝпјҢйңҖй…ҚеҗҲи¶ӢеҠҝиҝҮж»ӨгҖӮ
   9вҶ’"""
  10вҶ’
  11вҶ’from __future__ import annotations
  12вҶ’
  13вҶ’import pandas as pd
  14вҶ’
  15вҶ’from mytrader.strategy.indicators import rsi
  16вҶ’from mytrader.strategy.registry import register_strategy
  17вҶ’
  18вҶ’
  19вҶ’@register_strategy("rsi_mean_revert")
  20вҶ’def rsi_signal(
  21вҶ’    close: pd.Series,
  22вҶ’    period: int = 14,
  23вҶ’    oversold: float = 30.0,
  24вҶ’    overbought: float = 70.0,
  25вҶ’) -> pd.Series:
  26вҶ’    """RSI и¶…д№°и¶…еҚ–дҝЎеҸ·гҖӮ
  27вҶ’
  28вҶ’    Args:
  29вҶ’        close:      ж”¶зӣҳд»· Series
  30вҶ’        period:     RSI и®Ўз®—е‘ЁжңҹпјҲй»ҳи®Ө 14пјү
  31вҶ’        oversold:   и¶…еҚ–йҳҲеҖјпјҢдҪҺдәҺжӯӨеҖјеҸ‘еҮә BUYпјҲй»ҳи®Ө 30пјү
  32вҶ’        overbought: и¶…д№°йҳҲеҖјпјҢй«ҳдәҺжӯӨеҖјеҸ‘еҮә SELLпјҲй»ҳи®Ө 70пјү
  33вҶ’
  34вҶ’    Returns:
  35вҶ’        дҝЎеҸ· Seriesпјҡ1=BUY, -1=SELL, 0=HOLD
  36вҶ’    """
  37вҶ’    rsi_values = rsi(close, period)
  38вҶ’
  39вҶ’    signal = pd.Series(0, index=close.index, dtype=int)
  40вҶ’    signal[rsi_values < oversold]   =  1   # BUY
  41вҶ’    signal[rsi_values > overbought] = -1   # SELL
  42вҶ’
  43вҶ’    # вҡ пёҸ shift(1) йҒҝе…ҚеүҚи§ҶеҒҸе·®
  44вҶ’    return signal.shift(1).fillna(0).astype(int)
  45вҶ’   1вҶ’"""RSI еқҮеҖјеӣһеҪ’зӯ–з•ҘгҖӮ
   2вҶ’
   3вҶ’дҝЎеҸ·и§„еҲҷпјҡ
   4вҶ’    - RSI < oversoldпјҲй»ҳи®Ө 30пјүвҶ’ и¶…еҚ–пјҢBUY  (+1)
   5вҶ’    - RSI > overboughtпјҲй»ҳи®Ө 70пјүвҶ’ и¶…д№°пјҢSELL (-1)
   6вҶ’    - еҗҰеҲҷ                      вҶ’ HOLD  (0)
   7вҶ’
   8вҶ’йҖӮз”ЁеңәжҷҜпјҡйңҮиҚЎеёӮпјӣеҚ•иҫ№и¶ӢеҠҝдёӯдјҡйў‘з№ҒйҖҶеҠҝпјҢйңҖй…ҚеҗҲи¶ӢеҠҝиҝҮж»ӨгҖӮ
   9вҶ’"""
  10вҶ’
  11вҶ’from __future__ import annotations
  12вҶ’
  13вҶ’import pandas as pd
  14вҶ’
  15вҶ’from mytrader.strategy.indicators import rsi
  16вҶ’from mytrader.strategy.registry import register_strategy
  17вҶ’
  18вҶ’
  19вҶ’@register_strategy("rsi_mean_revert")
  20вҶ’def rsi_signal(
  21вҶ’    close: pd.Series,
  22вҶ’    period: int = 14,
  23вҶ’    oversold: float = 30.0,
  24вҶ’    overbought: float = 70.0,
  25вҶ’) -> pd.Series:
  26вҶ’    """RSI и¶…д№°и¶…еҚ–дҝЎеҸ·гҖӮ
  27вҶ’
  28вҶ’    Args:
  29вҶ’        close:      ж”¶зӣҳд»· Series
  30вҶ’        period:     RSI и®Ўз®—е‘ЁжңҹпјҲй»ҳи®Ө 14пјү
  31вҶ’        oversold:   и¶…еҚ–йҳҲеҖјпјҢдҪҺдәҺжӯӨеҖјеҸ‘еҮә BUYпјҲй»ҳи®Ө 30пјү
  32вҶ’        overbought: и¶…д№°йҳҲеҖјпјҢй«ҳдәҺжӯӨеҖјеҸ‘еҮә SELLпјҲй»ҳи®Ө 70пјү
  33вҶ’
  34вҶ’    Returns:
  35вҶ’        дҝЎеҸ· Seriesпјҡ1=BUY, -1=SELL, 0=HOLD
  36вҶ’    """
  37вҶ’    rsi_values = rsi(close, period)
  38вҶ’
  39вҶ’    signal = pd.Series(0, index=close.index, dtype=int)
  40вҶ’    signal[rsi_values < oversold]   =  1   # BUY
  41вҶ’    signal[rsi_values > overbought] = -1   # SELL
  42вҶ’
  43вҶ’    # вҡ пёҸ shift(1) йҒҝе…ҚеүҚи§ҶеҒҸе·®
  44вҶ’    return signal.shift(1).fillna(0).astype(int)
  45вҶ’Now I see a critical bug. In `main.py` line 313:
```python
strategies = ["dual_ma", "rsi", "macd", "bollinger"]
```

But in `registry.py`, the strategies are registered as `rsi_mean_revert`, `macd_cross`, `bollinger_band` (based on the filenames in strategies/ folder):
- `dual_ma.py` вҶ’ `@register_strategy("dual_ma")` вң“
- `rsi_mean_revert.py` вҶ’ `@register_strategy("rsi_mean_revert")` вҖ” NOT "rsi"
- `macd_cross.py` вҶ’ `@register_strategy("macd_cross")` вҖ” NOT "macd"
- `bollinger_band.py` вҶ’ `@register_strategy("bollinger_band")` вҖ” NOT "bollinger"

Let me verify this by checking the registry and the other strategy files. This is likely the reason why `strategy_weights.json` only contains `dual_ma` вҖ” the other 3 strategies failed to load silently (`_backtest_one` returns None when strategy_fn is not found, just logs debug).

This is a BUG (not changing strategy logic = low risk per L8).    8вҶ’

  10вҶ’

  12вҶ’
  13вҶ’# зӯ–з•ҘеҮҪж•°зӯҫеҗҚпјҡ(close: pd.Series, **params) -> pd.Series
  14вҶ’# иҝ”еӣһзҡ„ pd.Seriesпјҡ1=BUY, -1=SELL, 0=HOLDпјҢзҙўеј•дёҺ close зӣёеҗҢ
  15вҶ’StrategyFn = Callable[..., pd.Series]
  16вҶ’
  17вҶ’STRATEGY_REGISTRY: dict[str, StrategyFn] = {}
  18вҶ’
  19вҶ’
  20вҶ’def register_strategy(name: str) -> Callable[[StrategyFn], StrategyFn]:
  21вҶ’    """зӯ–з•ҘжіЁеҶҢиЈ…йҘ°еҷЁгҖӮ
  22вҶ’
  23вҶ’    Example::
  24вҶ’
  25вҶ’        @register_strategy("my_strategy")
  26вҶ’        def my_strategy(close: pd.Series, period: int = 14) -> pd.Series:
  27вҶ’            ...
  28вҶ’    """
  29вҶ’    def decorator(fn: StrategyFn) -> StrategyFn:
  30вҶ’        if name in STRATEGY_REGISTRY:
  31вҶ’            raise ValueError(f"Strategy '{name}' is already registered")
  32вҶ’        STRATEGY_REGISTRY[name] = fn
  33вҶ’        return fn
  34вҶ’
  35вҶ’    return decorator
  36вҶ’   1вҶ’"""зӯ–з•ҘжіЁеҶҢиЎЁгҖӮ

   9вҶ’"""

  14вҶ’
  15вҶ’from mytrader.strategy.indicators import macd, crossed_above, crossed_below
  16вҶ’from mytrader.strategy.registry import register_strategy
  17вҶ’

  19вҶ’@register_strategy("macd_cross")
  20вҶ’def macd_signal(
  21вҶ’    close: pd.Series,
  22вҶ’    fast: int = 12,
  23вҶ’    slow: int = 26,
  24вҶ’    signal_period: int = 9,
  25вҶ’) -> pd.Series:
  26вҶ’    """MACD дҝЎеҸ·зәҝдәӨеҸүдҝЎеҸ·гҖӮ
  27вҶ’
  28вҶ’    Args:
  29вҶ’        close:         ж”¶зӣҳд»· Series
  30вҶ’        fast:          еҝ«зәҝ EMA е‘ЁжңҹпјҲй»ҳи®Ө 12пјү
  31вҶ’        slow:          ж…ўзәҝ EMA е‘ЁжңҹпјҲй»ҳи®Ө 26пјү
  32вҶ’        signal_period: дҝЎеҸ·зәҝ EMA е‘ЁжңҹпјҲй»ҳи®Ө 9пјү
  33вҶ’
  34вҶ’    Returns:
  35вҶ’        дҝЎеҸ· Seriesпјҡ1=BUY, -1=SELL, 0=HOLD
  36вҶ’    """
  37вҶ’    macd_line, signal_line, _ = macd(close, fast, slow, signal_period)
  38вҶ’
  39вҶ’    buy_signal  = crossed_above(macd_line, signal_line).astype(int)
  40вҶ’    sell_signal = crossed_below(macd_line, signal_line).astype(int)
  41вҶ’
  42вҶ’    signal = buy_signal - sell_signal
  43вҶ’
  44вҶ’    # вҡ пёҸ shift(1) йҒҝе…ҚеүҚи§ҶеҒҸе·®
  45вҶ’    return signal.shift(1).fillna(0).astype(int)

  35вҶ’    """

  40вҶ’    signal[close > upper] = -1   # зӘҒз ҙдёҠиҪЁ вҶ’ SELL

"""зӯ–з•ҘжіЁеҶҢиЎЁгҖӮ

дҪҝз”Ё @register_strategy("name") иЈ…йҘ°еҷЁжіЁеҶҢзӯ–з•ҘеҮҪж•°пјҢ
йҖҡиҝҮ STRATEGY_REGISTRY["name"] иҺ·еҸ–еҜ№еә”еҮҪж•°гҖӮ
"""

from __future__ import annotations

from typing import Callable

import pandas as pd

# зӯ–з•ҘеҮҪж•°зӯҫеҗҚпјҡ(close: pd.Series, **params) -> pd.Series
# иҝ”еӣһзҡ„ pd.Seriesпјҡ1=BUY, -1=SELL, 0=HOLDпјҢзҙўеј•дёҺ close зӣёеҗҢ
StrategyFn = Callable[..., pd.Series]

STRATEGY_REGISTRY: dict[str, StrategyFn] = {}


def register_strategy(name: str) -> Callable[[StrategyFn], StrategyFn]:
    """зӯ–з•ҘжіЁеҶҢиЈ…йҘ°еҷЁгҖӮ

    Example::

        @register_strategy("my_strategy")
        def my_strategy(close: pd.Series, period: int = 14) -> pd.Series:
            ...
    """
    def decorator(fn: StrategyFn) -> StrategyFn:
        if name in STRATEGY_REGISTRY:
            raise ValueError(f"Strategy '{name}' is already registered")
        STRATEGY_REGISTRY[name] = fn
        return fn

    return decorator

Signal: (none)CONFIRMED BUG! This is a significant finding.

The actual registered strategy names are:
- `dual_ma` (in dual_ma.py)
- `rsi_mean_revert` (in rsi_mean_revert.py)
- `macd_cross` (in macd_cross.py)
- `bollinger_band` (in bollinger_band.py)

But `main.py` line 313 uses:
```python
strategies = ["dual_ma", "rsi", "macd", "bollinger"]
```

So `STRATEGY_REGISTRY.get("rsi")` returns None, `STRATEGY_REGISTRY.get("macd")` returns None, `STRATEGY_REGISTRY.get("bollinger")` returns None.

In `_backtest_one`:
```python
strategy_fn = STRATEGY_REGISTRY.get(strategy_name)
if strategy_fn is None:
    return None  # SILENTLY RETURNS NONE
```

And in `_run_group`, the warning is just "no valid results". This means:
- 3 out of 4 strategies are being silently skipped
- Only `dual_ma` is actually being backtested
- The `strategy_weights.json` shows exactly this вҖ” all 6 groups have only `dual_ma`

This is a bug that doesn't change strategy logic (just fixes a name mismatch so the actual strategies get included). Per L8, "Bug дҝ®еӨҚпјҲдёҚж”№еҸҳзӯ–з•ҘйҖ»иҫ‘пјү" is LOW RISK and can be auto-deployed.

1. Look at the matrix_runner.py to see if it has the same bug (in live scan)
2. Look at the tests
3. Run the tests to confirm current state
4. Possibly run the reoptimize after fix to see new weights

  31вҶ’@dataclass
  32вҶ’class MatrixScanResult:
  33вҶ’    """еҚ•ж¬Ўзҹ©йҳөжү«жҸҸз»“жһңгҖӮ"""
  34вҶ’
  35вҶ’    signals: list[Signal] = field(default_factory=list)
  36вҶ’    symbol_count: int = 0
  37вҶ’    strategy_runs: int = 0
  38вҶ’    errors: dict[str, str] = field(default_factory=dict)
  39вҶ’
  40вҶ’    @property
  41вҶ’    def buy_signals(self) -> list[Signal]:
  42вҶ’        return [s for s in self.signals if s.direction == SignalDirection.BUY]
  43вҶ’
  44вҶ’    @property
  45вҶ’    def sell_signals(self) -> list[Signal]:
  46вҶ’        return [s for s in self.signals if s.direction == SignalDirection.SELL]
  47вҶ’
  48вҶ’
  49вҶ’class StrategyMatrixRunner:
  50вҶ’    """зӯ–з•Ҙзҹ©йҳөиҝҗиЎҢеҷЁгҖӮ
  51вҶ’
  52вҶ’    Args:
  53вҶ’        store:             MarketDataStore е®һдҫӢ
  54вҶ’        universe:          UniverseManager е®һдҫӢ
  55вҶ’        weights_file:      strategy_weights.json и·Ҝеҫ„
  56вҶ’        signal_valid_bars: дҝЎеҸ·жңүж•ҲжңҹпјҲbar ж•°пјүпјҢй»ҳи®Ө 3
  57вҶ’                           N=1 йҖҖеҢ–дёәеҸӘзңӢжңҖеҗҺдёҖж № barпјҲдёҘж јжЁЎејҸпјү
  58вҶ’    """
  59вҶ’
  60вҶ’    def __init__(
  61вҶ’        self,
  62вҶ’        store: MarketDataStore,
  63вҶ’        universe: UniverseManager,
  64вҶ’        weights_file: str | Path | None = None,
  65вҶ’        signal_valid_bars: int = 3,
  66вҶ’    ) -> None:
  67вҶ’        self._store = store
  68вҶ’        self._universe = universe
  69вҶ’        self._signal_valid_bars = signal_valid_bars
  70вҶ’
  71вҶ’        if weights_file is None:
  72вҶ’            weights_file = self._find_weights_file()
  73вҶ’        self._weights_file = Path(weights_file) if weights_file else None
  74вҶ’        self._weights: dict[str, list[dict[str, Any]]] = {}
  75вҶ’        self._load_weights()
  76вҶ’
  77вҶ’    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
  78вҶ’    # е…¬е…ұжҺҘеҸЈ
  79вҶ’    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
  80вҶ’
  81вҶ’    def run(
  82вҶ’        self,
  83вҶ’        lookback_days: int = 90,
  84вҶ’        max_workers: int = 8,
  85вҶ’    ) -> MatrixScanResult:
  86вҶ’        """еҜ№е…Ёж Үзҡ„жұ иҝҗиЎҢеҗ„иҮӘеҲҶз»„зҡ„зӯ–з•ҘпјҢиҫ“еҮәдҝЎеҸ·еҲ—иЎЁгҖӮ"""
  87вҶ’        symbols = self._universe.get_universe()
  88вҶ’        result = MatrixScanResult(symbol_count=len(symbols))
  89вҶ’
  90вҶ’        with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=max_workers) as executor:
  91вҶ’            futures = {
  92вҶ’                executor.submit(self.run_symbol, sym, lookback_days): sym
  93вҶ’                for sym in symbols
  94вҶ’            }
  95вҶ’            for future in as_completed(futures):
  96вҶ’                sym = futures[future]
  97вҶ’                try:
  98вҶ’                    sigs = future.result()
  99вҶ’                    result.signals.extend(sigs)
 100вҶ’                    result.strategy_runs += len(sigs) + 1  # иҝ‘дјј
 101вҶ’                except Exception as e:
 102вҶ’                    result.errors[sym] = str(e)
 103вҶ’                    logger.debug(f"[matrix] {sym} error: {e}")
 104вҶ’
 105вҶ’        logger.info(
 106вҶ’            f"[matrix] scan done: {result.symbol_count} symbols, "
 107вҶ’            f"{len(result.signals)} signals, {len(result.errors)} errors"
 108вҶ’        )
 109вҶ’        return result
 110вҶ’
 111вҶ’    def run_symbol(
 112вҶ’        self,
 113вҶ’        symbol: str,
 114вҶ’        lookback_days: int = 90,
 115вҶ’    ) -> list[Signal]:
 116вҶ’        """иҝҗиЎҢеҚ•еҸӘж Үзҡ„зҡ„жүҖжңүеҲҶй…Қзӯ–з•ҘгҖӮ"""
 117вҶ’        meta = self._universe.get_symbol_meta(symbol)
 118вҶ’        if meta is None:
 119вҶ’            return []
 120вҶ’
 121вҶ’        group_strategies = self._weights.get(meta.group_id, [])
 122вҶ’        if not group_strategies:
 123вҶ’            # жңӘжүҫеҲ°з»„жқғйҮҚ вҶ’ fallbackпјҡе°қиҜ• UNKNOWN жҲ–з©әеҲ—иЎЁ
 124вҶ’            logger.debug(f"[matrix] {symbol}: no strategies for group {meta.group_id}")
 125вҶ’            return []
 126вҶ’
 127вҶ’        df = self._store.get_latest_n_bars(symbol, n=lookback_days)
 128вҶ’        if df.empty or len(df) < 10:
 129вҶ’            return []
 130вҶ’
 131вҶ’        signals: list[Signal] = []
 132вҶ’        now = datetime.now(tz=timezone.utc)
 133вҶ’
 134вҶ’        for entry in group_strategies:
 135вҶ’            strategy_name = entry["strategy"]
 136вҶ’            params = entry.get("params", {})
 137вҶ’            weight = float(entry.get("weight", 1.0))
 138вҶ’
 139вҶ’            strategy_fn = STRATEGY_REGISTRY.get(strategy_name)
 140вҶ’            if strategy_fn is None:
 141вҶ’                logger.warning(f"[matrix] strategy '{strategy_name}' not in registry, skip")
 142вҶ’                continue
 143вҶ’
 144вҶ’            try:
 145вҶ’                # вҡ пёҸ дј е…Ҙе®Ңж•ҙ dfпјҲйғЁеҲҶзӯ–з•ҘйңҖ high/low/volumeпјү
 146вҶ’                sig_series = strategy_fn(df["close"], df=df, **params)
 147вҶ’            except TypeError:
 148вҶ’                # зӯ–з•ҘеҮҪж•°дёҚжҺҘеҸ— df еҸӮж•°ж—¶пјҢеҸӘдј  close
 149вҶ’                sig_series = strategy_fn(df["close"], **params)
 150вҶ’            except Exception as e:
 151вҶ’                logger.debug(f"[matrix] {symbol}/{strategy_name} error: {e}")
 152вҶ’                continue
 153вҶ’
 154вҶ’            # вҡ пёҸ дҝЎеҸ·жңүж•ҲжңҹпјҡжЈҖжҹҘжңҖиҝ‘ N bar еҶ…жҳҜеҗҰеҮәзҺ°иҝҮйқһйӣ¶дҝЎеҸ·
 155вҶ’            # и§ЈеҶідәӢд»¶еһӢдҝЎеҸ·пјҲйҮ‘еҸүеҸӘеңЁеҪ“еӨ©=1пјүеңЁйқһдҝЎеҸ·ж—Ҙиў«жјҸжҺүзҡ„й—®йўҳ
 156вҶ’            recent = sig_series.iloc[-self._signal_valid_bars :]
 157вҶ’            nonzero = recent[recent != 0]
 158вҶ’            if nonzero.empty:
 159вҶ’                continue
 160вҶ’
 161вҶ’            latest = int(nonzero.iloc[-1])  # еҸ–жңҖиҝ‘дёҖж¬Ўжңүж•ҲдҝЎеҸ·ж–№еҗ‘
 162вҶ’
 163вҶ’            direction = SignalDirection.BUY if latest == 1 else SignalDirection.SELL
 164вҶ’            confidence = min(weight, 1.0)
 165вҶ’
 166вҶ’            signals.append(
 167вҶ’                Signal(
 168вҶ’                    symbol=symbol,
 169вҶ’                    direction=direction,
 170вҶ’                    timestamp=now,
 171вҶ’                    confidence=confidence,
 172вҶ’                    strategy_name=strategy_name,
 173вҶ’                    indicators={
 174вҶ’                        "group_id": meta.group_id,
 175вҶ’                        "backtest_sharpe": entry.get("backtest_sharpe", 0.0),
 176вҶ’                        "backtest_win_rate": entry.get("backtest_win_rate", 0.0),
 177вҶ’                        "weight": weight,
 178вҶ’                    },
 179вҶ’                )
 180вҶ’            )
 181вҶ’
 182вҶ’        return signals
 183вҶ’
 184вҶ’    def reload_weights(self) -> None:
 185вҶ’        """зғӯеҠ иҪҪ strategy_weights.jsonпјҲжҜҸжңҲ MatrixBacktest жӣҙж–°еҗҺж— йңҖйҮҚеҗҜпјүгҖӮ"""
 186вҶ’        self._load_weights()
 187вҶ’        logger.info("[matrix] weights reloaded")
 188вҶ’
 189вҶ’    def set_weights_for_group(
 190вҶ’        self, group_id: str, strategies: list[dict[str, Any]]
 191вҶ’    ) -> None:
 192вҶ’        """зӣҙжҺҘжіЁе…ҘеҲҶз»„жқғйҮҚпјҲжөӢиҜ•/и°ғиҜ•з”ЁпјүгҖӮ"""
 193вҶ’        self._weights[group_id] = strategies

 195вҶ’    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
 196вҶ’    # еҶ…йғЁж–№жі•
 197вҶ’    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
 198вҶ’
 199вҶ’    def _load_weights(self) -> None:
 200вҶ’        """д»Һ JSON ж–Үд»¶еҠ иҪҪзӯ–з•ҘжқғйҮҚгҖӮ"""
 201вҶ’        if self._weights_file and self._weights_file.exists():
 202вҶ’            with open(self._weights_file, encoding="utf-8") as f:
 203вҶ’                data = json.load(f)
 204вҶ’            self._weights = data.get("groups", {})
 205вҶ’            logger.info(
 206вҶ’                f"[matrix] weights loaded: {len(self._weights)} groups from {self._weights_file}"
 207вҶ’            )
 208вҶ’        else:
 209вҶ’            self._weights = {}
 210вҶ’            logger.debug("[matrix] no weights file, using empty weights")
 211вҶ’
 212вҶ’    @staticmethod
 213вҶ’    def _find_weights_file() -> Path | None:
 214вҶ’        """д»Һ cwd еҗ‘дёҠжҹҘжүҫ config/strategy_weights.jsonгҖӮ"""
 215вҶ’        here = Path.cwd()
 216вҶ’        for parent in [here, *here.parents]:
 217вҶ’            candidate = parent / "config" / "strategy_weights.json"
 218вҶ’            if candidate.exists():
 219вҶ’                return candidate
 220вҶ’        return None

  33вҶ’    """еҚ•ж¬Ўзҹ©йҳөжү«жҸҸз»“жһңгҖӮ"""
  34вҶ’
  35вҶ’    signals: list[Signal] = field(default_factory=list)
  36вҶ’    symbol_count: int = 0
  37вҶ’    strategy_runs: int = 0
  38вҶ’    errors: dict[str, str] = field(default_factory=dict)
  39вҶ’
  40вҶ’    @property
  41вҶ’    def buy_signals(self) -> list[Signal]:
  42вҶ’        return [s for s in self.signals if s.direction == SignalDirection.BUY]
  43вҶ’
  44вҶ’    @property
  45вҶ’    def sell_signals(self) -> list[Signal]:
  46вҶ’        return [s for s in self.signals if s.direction == SignalDirection.SELL]
  47вҶ’
  48вҶ’
  49вҶ’class StrategyMatrixRunner:
  50вҶ’    """зӯ–з•Ҙзҹ©йҳөиҝҗиЎҢеҷЁгҖӮ
  51вҶ’
  52вҶ’    Args:
  53вҶ’        store:             MarketDataStore е®һдҫӢ
  54вҶ’        universe:          UniverseManager е®һдҫӢ
  55вҶ’        weights_file:      strategy_weights.json и·Ҝеҫ„
  56вҶ’        signal_valid_bars: дҝЎеҸ·жңүж•ҲжңҹпјҲbar ж•°пјүпјҢй»ҳи®Ө 3
  57вҶ’                           N=1 йҖҖеҢ–дёәеҸӘзңӢжңҖеҗҺдёҖж № barпјҲдёҘж јжЁЎејҸпјү
  58вҶ’    """
  59вҶ’
  60вҶ’    def __init__(
  61вҶ’        self,
  62вҶ’        store: MarketDataStore,
  63вҶ’        universe: UniverseManager,
  64вҶ’        weights_file: str | Path | None = None,
  65вҶ’        signal_valid_bars: int = 3,
  66вҶ’    ) -> None:
  67вҶ’        self._store = store
  68вҶ’        self._universe = universe
  69вҶ’        self._signal_valid_bars = signal_valid_bars
  70вҶ’
  71вҶ’        if weights_file is None:
  72вҶ’            weights_file = self._find_weights_file()
  73вҶ’        self._weights_file = Path(weights_file) if weights_file else None
  74вҶ’        self._weights: dict[str, list[dict[str, Any]]] = {}
  75вҶ’        self._load_weights()
  76вҶ’
  77вҶ’    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
  78вҶ’    # е…¬е…ұжҺҘеҸЈ
  79вҶ’    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
  80вҶ’
  81вҶ’    def run(
  82вҶ’        self,
  83вҶ’        lookback_days: int = 90,
  84вҶ’        max_workers: int = 8,
  85вҶ’    ) -> MatrixScanResult:
  86вҶ’        """еҜ№е…Ёж Үзҡ„жұ иҝҗиЎҢеҗ„иҮӘеҲҶз»„зҡ„зӯ–з•ҘпјҢиҫ“еҮәдҝЎеҸ·еҲ—иЎЁгҖӮ"""
  87вҶ’        symbols = self._universe.get_universe()
  88вҶ’        result = MatrixScanResult(symbol_count=len(symbols))
  89вҶ’
  90вҶ’        with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=max_workers) as executor:
  91вҶ’            futures = {
  92вҶ’                executor.submit(self.run_symbol, sym, lookback_days): sym
  93вҶ’                for sym in symbols
  94вҶ’            }
  95вҶ’            for future in as_completed(futures):
  96вҶ’                sym = futures[future]
  97вҶ’                try:
  98вҶ’                    sigs = future.result()
  99вҶ’                    result.signals.extend(sigs)
 100вҶ’                    result.strategy_runs += len(sigs) + 1  # иҝ‘дјј
 101вҶ’                except Exception as e:
 102вҶ’                    result.errors[sym] = str(e)
 103вҶ’                    logger.debug(f"[matrix] {sym} error: {e}")
 104вҶ’
 105вҶ’        logger.info(
 106вҶ’            f"[matrix] scan done: {result.symbol_count} symbols, "
 107вҶ’            f"{len(result.signals)} signals, {len(result.errors)} errors"
 108вҶ’        )
 109вҶ’        return result
 110вҶ’
 111вҶ’    def run_symbol(
 112вҶ’        self,
 113вҶ’        symbol: str,
 114вҶ’        lookback_days: int = 90,
 115вҶ’    ) -> list[Signal]:
 116вҶ’        """иҝҗиЎҢеҚ•еҸӘж Үзҡ„зҡ„жүҖжңүеҲҶй…Қзӯ–з•ҘгҖӮ"""
 117вҶ’        meta = self._universe.get_symbol_meta(symbol)
 118вҶ’        if meta is None:
 119вҶ’            return []
 120вҶ’
 121вҶ’        group_strategies = self._weights.get(meta.group_id, [])
 122вҶ’        if not group_strategies:
 123вҶ’            # жңӘжүҫеҲ°з»„жқғйҮҚ вҶ’ fallbackпјҡе°қиҜ• UNKNOWN жҲ–з©әеҲ—иЎЁ
 124вҶ’            logger.debug(f"[matrix] {symbol}: no strategies for group {meta.group_id}")
 125вҶ’            return []
 126вҶ’
 127вҶ’        df = self._store.get_latest_n_bars(symbol, n=lookback_days)
 128вҶ’        if df.empty or len(df) < 10:
 129вҶ’            return []
 130вҶ’
 131вҶ’        signals: list[Signal] = []
 132вҶ’        now = datetime.now(tz=timezone.utc)
 133вҶ’
 134вҶ’        for entry in group_strategies:
 135вҶ’            strategy_name = entry["strategy"]
 136вҶ’            params = entry.get("params", {})
 137вҶ’            weight = float(entry.get("weight", 1.0))
 138вҶ’
 139вҶ’            strategy_fn = STRATEGY_REGISTRY.get(strategy_name)
 140вҶ’            if strategy_fn is None:
 141вҶ’                logger.warning(f"[matrix] strategy '{strategy_name}' not in registry, skip")
 142вҶ’                continue
 143вҶ’
 144вҶ’            try:
 145вҶ’                # вҡ пёҸ дј е…Ҙе®Ңж•ҙ dfпјҲйғЁеҲҶзӯ–з•ҘйңҖ high/low/volumeпјү
 146вҶ’                sig_series = strategy_fn(df["close"], df=df, **params)
 147вҶ’            except TypeError:
 148вҶ’                # зӯ–з•ҘеҮҪж•°дёҚжҺҘеҸ— df еҸӮж•°ж—¶пјҢеҸӘдј  close
 149вҶ’                sig_series = strategy_fn(df["close"], **params)
 150вҶ’            except Exception as e:
 151вҶ’                logger.debug(f"[matrix] {symbol}/{strategy_name} error: {e}")
 152вҶ’                continue
 153вҶ’
 154вҶ’            # вҡ пёҸ дҝЎеҸ·жңүж•ҲжңҹпјҡжЈҖжҹҘжңҖиҝ‘ N bar еҶ…жҳҜеҗҰеҮәзҺ°иҝҮйқһйӣ¶дҝЎеҸ·
 155вҶ’            # и§ЈеҶідәӢд»¶еһӢдҝЎеҸ·пјҲйҮ‘еҸүеҸӘеңЁеҪ“еӨ©=1пјүеңЁйқһдҝЎеҸ·ж—Ҙиў«жјҸжҺүзҡ„й—®йўҳ
 156вҶ’            recent = sig_series.iloc[-self._signal_valid_bars :]
 157вҶ’            nonzero = recent[recent != 0]
 158вҶ’            if nonzero.empty:
 159вҶ’                continue
 160вҶ’
 161вҶ’            latest = int(nonzero.iloc[-1])  # еҸ–жңҖиҝ‘дёҖж¬Ўжңүж•ҲдҝЎеҸ·ж–№еҗ‘
 162вҶ’
 163вҶ’            direction = SignalDirection.BUY if latest == 1 else SignalDirection.SELL
 164вҶ’            confidence = min(weight, 1.0)
 165вҶ’
 166вҶ’            signals.append(
 167вҶ’                Signal(
 168вҶ’                    symbol=symbol,
 169вҶ’                    direction=direction,
 170вҶ’                    timestamp=now,
 171вҶ’                    confidence=confidence,
 172вҶ’                    strategy_name=strategy_name,
 173вҶ’                    indicators={
 174вҶ’                        "group_id": meta.group_id,
 175вҶ’                        "backtest_sharpe": entry.get("backtest_sharpe", 0.0),
 176вҶ’                        "backtest_win_rate": entry.get("backtest_win_rate", 0.0),
 177вҶ’                        "weight": weight,
 178вҶ’                    },
 179вҶ’                )
 180вҶ’            )
 181вҶ’
 182вҶ’        return signals
 183вҶ’
 184вҶ’    def reload_weights(self) -> None:
 185вҶ’        """зғӯеҠ иҪҪ strategy_weights.jsonпјҲжҜҸжңҲ MatrixBacktest жӣҙж–°еҗҺж— йңҖйҮҚеҗҜпјүгҖӮ"""
 186вҶ’        self._load_weights()
 187вҶ’        logger.info("[matrix] weights reloaded")
 188вҶ’
 189вҶ’    def set_weights_for_group(
 190вҶ’        self, group_id: str, strategies: list[dict[str, Any]]
 191вҶ’    ) -> None:
 192вҶ’        """зӣҙжҺҘжіЁе…ҘеҲҶз»„жқғйҮҚпјҲжөӢиҜ•/и°ғиҜ•з”ЁпјүгҖӮ"""
 193вҶ’        self._weights[group_id] = strategies
 194вҶ’
 195вҶ’    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
 196вҶ’    # еҶ…йғЁж–№жі•
 197вҶ’    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
 198вҶ’
 199вҶ’    def _load_weights(self) -> None:
 200вҶ’        """д»Һ JSON ж–Үд»¶еҠ иҪҪзӯ–з•ҘжқғйҮҚгҖӮ"""
 201вҶ’        if self._weights_file and self._weights_file.exists():
 202вҶ’            with open(self._weights_file, encoding="utf-8") as f:
 203вҶ’                data = json.load(f)
 204вҶ’            self._weights = data.get("groups", {})
 205вҶ’            logger.info(
 206вҶ’                f"[matrix] weights loaded: {len(self._weights)} groups from {self._weights_file}"
 207вҶ’            )
 208вҶ’        else:
 209вҶ’            self._weights = {}
 210вҶ’            logger.debug("[matrix] no weights file, using empty weights")
 211вҶ’
 212вҶ’    @staticmethod
 213вҶ’    def _find_weights_file() -> Path | None:
 214вҶ’        """д»Һ cwd еҗ‘дёҠжҹҘжүҫ config/strategy_weights.jsonгҖӮ"""
 215вҶ’        here = Path.cwd()
 216вҶ’        for parent in [here, *here.parents]:
 217вҶ’            candidate = parent / "config" / "strategy_weights.json"
 218вҶ’            if candidate.exists():
 219вҶ’                return candidate
 220вҶ’        return None

Now I have all the context I need. Let me summarize the findings and confirm:

**Confirmed Bugs:**

1. **BUG #1 (Critical)**: `main.py:313-318` uses wrong strategy names
   - Uses: `["dual_ma", "rsi", "macd", "bollinger"]`
   - Should be: `["dual_ma", "rsi_mean_revert", "macd_cross", "bollinger_band"]`
   - **Impact**: 3 out of 4 strategies silently skipped in `--reoptimize` вҶ’ strategy_weights.json only contains dual_ma вҶ’ StrategyMatrixRunner only runs dual_ma in live scan вҶ’ ensemble is effectively single-strategy
   - This is a **bug fix** (L8 low risk)

2. **BUG #2**: `examples/phase5_e2e.py:76` uses `"macd"` instead of `"macd_cross"` вҖ” same bug in example script

3. **Secondary observations**:
   - Param grids are tiny: rsi `{period:[14], oversold:[30], overbought:[70]}` = single point, no grid search
   - macd: `{fast:[12], slow:[26], signal_period:[9]}` = single point
   - bollinger: `{period:[20], std_dev:[2.0]}` = single point
   - Only dual_ma has real grid: `{fast:[5,10], slow:[20,40,60]}` = 6 combos
   - Even after fixing names, 3 strategies will only be tested at default params
   - But this is a separate (smaller) issue вҖ” let me note it but focus on the critical bug first

4. **Noisy backtest results**:
   - Phase 1 dev records show on AAPL 2022-2025:
     - bollinger: +44.5%, Sharpe 0.96, MaxDD 20.5%
     - macd: +36.9%, Sharpe 0.87, MaxDD 20.0%
     - rsi: +19.3%, Sharpe 0.47, MaxDD 26.0%
     - dual_ma: +15.9%, Sharpe 0.46, MaxDD 20.7%
     - buy&hold: +39.8%
   - So rsi has MaxDD 26% (> 20% constraint!), others OK
   - bollinger actually beats buy&hold on AAPL
   - But these are single-symbol results, not the matrix

5. **Sortino missing**: MatrixBacktest only computes Sharpe, not Sortino. Constitution says "йҰ–иҰҒ KPI: Sortino жҜ”зҺҮ". This is a gap вҖ” but expanding to compute Sortino would be adding functionality (could be low-risk addition: it's a metric, not changing strategy logic). Let me consider whether to include this.

6. **No `_backtest_one` test for missing strategy**: tests/test_matrix_backtest.py tests only dual_ma and "rsi" (line 207-210) вҖ” but the test expects `rsi` to work! Let me check that test.

  70вҶ’            "[runner] strategy_weights.json not found, injecting default weights for demo"
  71вҶ’        )
  72вҶ’        # еҗ‘жүҖжңүеҲҶз»„жіЁе…Ҙй»ҳи®ӨжқғйҮҚпјҲжј”зӨәз”Ёпјү
  73вҶ’        default_strategies = [
  74вҶ’            {"strategy": "dual_ma",  "params": {"fast": 5, "slow": 60},

  79вҶ’        for gid in groups:
  80вҶ’            runner.set_weights_for_group(gid, default_strategies)

  84вҶ’    # 4. зҹ©йҳөжү«жҸҸ

 100вҶ’Now I see the full picture. The `test_run_weights_sum_to_one` test uses `strategies=["dual_ma", "rsi"]` with `param_grids` containing `"rsi"` вҖ” but registry has `"rsi_mean_revert"`. This means the test ALSO has the bug вҖ” it passes simply because:
- `dual_ma` works fine
- `rsi` silently fails (returns None in `_backtest_one`), so it's filtered out in `_run_group`
- Only `dual_ma` produces results, so weight = 1.0 (single strategy)
- The test asserts "weights sum to 1.0" which trivially passes with a single strategy

So the tests don't catch this bug. This is a classic case where the test has the same bug as the code.

# Phase 1 вҖ” зҺ°зҠ¶еҲҶжһҗ

## 1. еҪ“еүҚејҖеҸ‘йҳ¶ж®ө
**Phase 5 е®ҢжҲҗпјҢPhase 6 еҫ…ејҖеҸ‘**гҖӮ467 tests passedгҖӮеҸҢеұӮжһ¶жһ„пјҲзҰ»зәҝзҹ©йҳөеӣһжөӢ + еңЁзәҝзҹ©йҳөжү«жҸҸпјүеҹәзЎҖи®ҫж–Ҫе·Іе°ұз»ӘпјҢдҪҶ**еңЁзәҝеұӮе®һйҷ…еҸӘи·‘дәҶ 1 дёӘзӯ–з•Ҙ**пјҲиҜҰи§ҒдёӢж–ҮпјүгҖӮ

## 2. зҰ»зӣ®ж Үзҡ„и·қзҰ»
| з»ҙеәҰ | Constitution зӣ®ж Ү | еҪ“еүҚзҠ¶жҖҒ | е·®и·қ |
|------|------------------|---------|------|
| е№ҙеҢ–ж”¶зӣҠ | 20-30%пјҲеә•зәҝ 10%пјү | зҹ©йҳөеӣһжөӢз»„еҗҲ Sharpe 0.07-0.95пјҢдҪҺжіўеҠЁз»„жҺҘиҝ‘еҷӘеЈ° | **дёҘйҮҚдёҚи¶і** |
| жңҖеӨ§еӣһж’Ө | вүӨ 20%пјҲзЎ¬зәҰжқҹпјү | Phase 1 еҚ•ж Үзҡ„жөӢиҜ•пјҡrsi 26%гҖҒbollinger 20.5%гҖҒdual_ma 20.7% | еӨҡдёӘзӯ–з•Ҙ**зӘҒз ҙзәҰжқҹ** |
| SortinoпјҲйҰ–иҰҒ KPIпјү | дјҳеҢ–зӣ®ж Ү | **е®Ңе…ЁжңӘи®Ўз®—**пјҢд»Јз ҒйҮҢеҸӘжңү Sharpe | **еҹәзЎҖи®ҫж–ҪзјәеӨұ** |
| CalmarпјҲж¬ЎиҰҒ KPIпјү | и·ҹиёӘ | жңӘи®Ўз®— | зјәеӨұ |

## 3. еӣӣзӯ–з•ҘеӣһжөӢиЎЁзҺ°пјҲPhase 1 и®°еҪ•пјҢAAPL 2022-2025 еҚ•ж Үзҡ„пјү
| зӯ–з•Ҙ | жҖ»еӣһжҠҘ | Sharpe | MaxDD | з“¶йўҲ |
|------|--------|--------|-------|------|
| bollinger | +44.5% | 0.96 | 20.5% | DD з•Ҙи¶…зәҰжқҹ |
| macd | +36.9% | 0.87 | 20.0% | иҫҫж ҮдҪҶж”¶зӣҠдёҖиҲ¬ |
| rsi | +19.3% | 0.47 | **26.0%** | DD дёҘйҮҚи¶…ж Ү |
| dual_ma | +15.9% | 0.46 | 20.7% | ж”¶зӣҠ/Sharpe еҸҢдҪҺ |
| buy&hold | +39.8% | вҖ” | вҖ” | еҹәеҮҶ |

**дҪҶдёҠиЎЁжҳҜиҜҜеҜјжҖ§зҡ„**вҖ”вҖ”еӣ дёә `main.py:313` зҡ„зӯ–з•ҘеҗҚ bugпјҢзҹ©йҳөеӣһжөӢ**е®һйҷ…еҸӘи·‘дәҶ dual_ma**пјҲе…¶дҪҷ 3 дёӘиў« `_backtest_one` йқҷй»ҳи·іиҝҮпјүгҖӮ`strategy_weights.json` 6 дёӘз»„**е…ЁйғЁеҸӘеү© dual_ma**е°ұжҳҜй“ҒиҜҒгҖӮжүҖд»Ҙзңҹе®һзҡ„зҹ©йҳө ensemble иЎЁзҺ° = д»… dual_maпјҢжҳҜ 4 дёӘзӯ–з•ҘйҮҢ**жңҖе·®зҡ„йӮЈдёӘ**гҖӮ

## 4. еҹәзЎҖи®ҫж–Ҫе°ұз»ӘеәҰ
| жЁЎеқ— | зҠ¶жҖҒ | иҜҙжҳҺ |
|------|------|------|
| MarketDataStore | вң… еҸҜз”Ё | жң¬ең° DB 85MBпјҢ604 еҸӘж Үзҡ„пјҢ5 е№ҙж•°жҚ® |
| UniverseManager | вң… еҸҜз”Ё | 6 з»„жіўеҠЁзҺҮеҲҶеұӮе·Із”ҹжҲҗ |
| MatrixBacktest | вҡ пёҸ жңү bug | жЎҶжһ¶жӯЈзЎ®пјҢдҪҶи°ғз”Ёж–№дј й”ҷзӯ–з•ҘеҗҚпјӣдё”д»…з®— Sharpe дёҚз®— Sortino |
| Walk-Forward | вң… еҸҜз”Ё | и°ғеәҰеҷЁжҜҸжңҲи§ҰеҸ‘е·ІжҺҘе…Ҙ |
| **е…ій”® bug** | вқҢ | `_run_group` еҜ№жүҫдёҚеҲ°зҡ„зӯ–з•Ҙ**йқҷй»ҳ return None**пјҢж—  warningпјҢеҜјиҮҙ bug йҡҗи—Ҹ 6 еӨ©пјҲ6-24 дә§еҮә weights иҮід»Ҡпјү |

## 5. жң¬иҪ®иҝӯд»ЈжңҖиҜҘдјҳе…Ҳи§ЈеҶід»Җд№Ҳ

**дҝ®еӨҚ MatrixBacktest зӯ–з•ҘеҗҚдёҚеҢ№й…Қ bug**гҖӮзҗҶз”ұпјҡ
1. **жқ жқҶжңҖй«ҳ**пјҡи§Јй”Ғ 75% иў«еұҸи”Ҫзҡ„зӯ–з•Ҙз©әй—ҙпјҲ4 дёӘзӯ–з•ҘйҮҢ 3 дёӘжІЎи·‘пјүпјҢжҳҜжүҖжңүе…¶д»–дјҳеҢ–зҡ„еүҚжҸҗ
2. **йӣ¶зӯ–з•ҘйҖ»иҫ‘еҸҳжӣҙ**пјҡзәҜ bug fixпјҢеұһ L8 дҪҺйЈҺйҷ©пјҢеҸҜиҮӘеҠЁйғЁзҪІ
3. **зӣҙжҺҘжңҚеҠЎйҰ–иҰҒ KPI**пјҡbug дёҚдҝ®пјҢд»»дҪ•еҸӮж•°и°ғдјҳ/ж–°зӯ–з•Ҙиҝӯд»ЈйғҪеңЁ"д»… dual_ma"зҡ„й”ҷиҜҜеҹәеҮҶдёҠеҒҡеҲӨж–ӯ
4. **йҷ„еёҰиЎҘйҪҗеҹәзЎҖи®ҫж–Ҫ**пјҡиЎҘ Sortino и®Ўз®—пјҲConstitution йҰ–иҰҒ KPI еҪ“еүҚзјәеӨұпјү+ иЎҘйқҷй»ҳеӨұиҙҘе‘ҠиӯҰпјҲйҳІжӯўеҗҢзұ» bug еҶҚи—Ҹ 6 еӨ©пјү

# Phase 2 вҖ” иҝӯд»Ји®ЎеҲ’

## иҝӯд»Ј #1 вҖ” дҝ®еӨҚ MatrixBacktest зӯ–з•ҘеҗҚдёҚеҢ№й…Қ Bug + еҗҜз”Ё Sortino жҢҮж Ү

- **зӣ®ж Ү**:
  1. `strategy_weights.json` йҮҚж–°з”ҹжҲҗеҗҺпјҢ6 дёӘз»„еҗ„иҮӘеҮәзҺ°зңҹе®һжңҖдјҳзҡ„зӯ–з•Ҙз»„еҗҲпјҲдёҚеҶҚе…ЁйғЁжҳҜ dual_maпјү
  2. зҹ©йҳөеӣһжөӢдә§еҮә Sortino жҢҮж ҮпјҲConstitution йҰ–иҰҒ KPIпјү
  3. еҗҢзұ»"зӯ–з•ҘеҗҚжӢјеҶҷй”ҷиҜҜ"жңӘжқҘдёҚеҶҚйқҷй»ҳеӨұиҙҘ
- **ж–№жЎҲ**:
  1. **Bug fix**: `main.py:313` зҡ„ `["dual_ma","rsi","macd","bollinger"]` вҶ’ `["dual_ma","rsi_mean_revert","macd_cross","bollinger_band"]`пјҢдёҺ `param_grids` keys еҗҢжӯҘ
  2. **Bug fix**: `examples/phase5_e2e.py:76` зҡ„ `"macd"` вҶ’ `"macd_cross"`
  3. **и§ӮжөӢжҖ§**: `matrix_backtest._run_group` еҜ№ `STRATEGY_REGISTRY.get(name) is None` ж”№дёә `logger.warning` + `continue`пјҲеҪ“еүҚжҳҜ `_backtest_one` еҶ…йғЁ debug зә§йқҷй»ҳ return Noneпјү
  4. **ж–°еўһжҢҮж Ү**: `matrix_backtest.py` еҠ  `_compute_sortino()`пјҢ`SingleBacktestResult.sortino`гҖҒ`GroupBacktestResult.portfolio_sortino` еӯ—ж®өпјҢweights JSON иҫ“еҮә `backtest_sortino`
  5. **жөӢиҜ•дҝ®еӨҚ**: `test_matrix_backtest.py::test_run_weights_sum_to_one` жҠҠ `"rsi"` ж”№жҲҗ `"rsi_mean_revert"`пјҲжөӢиҜ•жңүеҗҢж¬ҫ bugпјҢзў°е·§йҖҡиҝҮпјү
  6. **еӣһеҪ’жөӢиҜ•**: ж–°еўһ `test_reoptimize_strategy_names_match_registry` вҖ”вҖ” ж–ӯиЁҖ `main._run_reoptimize` з”Ёзҡ„зӯ–з•ҘеҗҚе…ЁйғЁеңЁ `STRATEGY_REGISTRY` дёӯпјҲйҳІеӣһеҪ’пјү
- **еҪұе“ҚиҢғеӣҙ**:
  - `mytrader/main.py`пјҲж”№ 4 иЎҢпјү
  - `mytrader/examples/phase5_e2e.py`пјҲж”№ 1 иЎҢпјү

  - `tests/test_matrix_backtest.py`пјҲдҝ® 1 жөӢиҜ• + еҠ  1 жөӢиҜ•пјү
  - `designs/design_v2/07-backtest-module.md`гҖҒ`12-strategy-matrix.md`гҖҒ`CHANGELOG.md`
  - йҮҚж–°з”ҹжҲҗ `config/strategy_weights.json`
- **йў„жңҹйЈҺйҷ©**:
  - йҮҚж–°и·‘ `--reoptimize` еҗҺйғЁеҲҶз»„зҡ„жңҖдјҳзӯ–з•ҘдјҡеҸҳпјҲdual_ma вҶ’ е…¶д»–пјүпјҢиҝҷжҳҜ**йў„жңҹиЎҢдёә**

- **йЈҺйҷ©зӯүзә§**: **дҪҺйЈҺйҷ©**пјҲL8: Bug дҝ®еӨҚдёҚж”№еҸҳзӯ–з•ҘйҖ»иҫ‘ + ж—Ҙеҝ—/зӣ‘жҺ§ж”№иҝӣ + ж–°еўһе·ІйӘҢиҜҒжҢҮж Үзҡ„еәҰйҮҸпјү

 130вҶ’    def test_backtest_one_with_open(self):
 131вҶ’Important вҖ” `SingleBacktestResult` is constructed positionally in tests:
```python
SingleBacktestResult("SYM1", "s1", {}, s1, 10, 5, 60, 20, r1)
```
This is `(symbol, strategy, params, sharpe, total_return_pct, max_drawdown_pct, win_rate_pct, total_trades, daily_returns)`.

If I add `sortino` as a NEW field, I need to add it with a default value (so positional construction still works). I should add it AFTER the existing fields with a default. Let me add `sortino: float = 0.0` after `daily_returns`. But wait вҖ” `daily_returns: pd.Series` has no default. If I add `sortino` after it with a default, that's fine (sortino gets default, daily_returns stays required positional).

Actually, to be safe and not break positional construction `SingleBacktestResult("SYM1", "s1", {}, s1, 10, 5, 60, 20, r1)`, I'll add `sortino` as a keyword field with default AFTER `daily_returns`:
```python
@dataclass
class SingleBacktestResult:
    symbol: str
    strategy: str
    params: dict
    sharpe: float
    total_return_pct: float
    max_drawdown_pct: float
    win_rate_pct: float
    total_trades: int
    daily_returns: pd.Series
    sortino: float = 0.0   # NEW, default 0.0, backward-compatible with positional construction
```

For `GroupBacktestResult`:
```python
@dataclass
class GroupBacktestResult:
    group_id: str
    strategy: str
    params: dict
    portfolio_sharpe: float
    avg_total_return_pct: float
    avg_max_drawdown_pct: float
    avg_win_rate_pct: float
    symbol_count: int
    portfolio_sortino: float = 0.0   # NEW
```

Now the Sortino computation. Standard formula:
- Sortino = (mean(returns) - risk_free_rate) / downside_deviation * sqrt(periods_per_year)
- risk_free_rate = 0 (simplify, consistent with Sharpe computation which uses mean/std with no rf)
- downside_deviation = sqrt(mean(min(0, returns - target)^2))
- target = 0 (or mean(returns))

Let me use target=0 (the common simplification), which matches the Sharpe computation's "no rf" assumption:
```python
def _compute_sortino(returns: pd.Series, periods_per_year: int = 252, target: float = 0.0) -> float:
    returns = returns.dropna()
    if len(returns) < 5:
        return 0.0
    downside = returns - target
    downside = downside.where(downside < 0, 0.0)  # only negative deviations
    # downside deviation = sqrt(mean(downside^2))
    dd = np.sqrt((downside ** 2).mean())
    if dd <= 0 or np.isnan(dd):
        return 0.0  # no downside вҶ’ infinite Sortino, but we return 0 to avoid inf
    mean = returns.mean()
    return float(mean / dd * np.sqrt(periods_per_year))
```

Wait вҖ” if there's no downside (all positive returns), Sortino should be +inf, not 0. Returning 0 is misleading. But returning inf breaks downstream arithmetic. Common practice: cap at a large value or return 0. Actually, for backtest comparison purposes, returning a large finite value is more honest. But for simplicity and to match `_compute_sharpe`'s "return 0 on degenerate" pattern, I'll return 0.0 and add a comment.

Hmm, actually the standard convention is:
- If std=0 in Sharpe вҶ’ undefined вҶ’ return 0 (current code does this)
- If downside_dev=0 in Sortino вҶ’ no downside вҶ’ very good вҶ’ return inf or large number

But for the matrix backtest weight computation, inf would break things. Let me return 0.0 for the degenerate case and add a docstring note. Actually вҖ” let me think about whether returning 0 is misleading. In a 5-year backtest with real data, there will always be some downside days, so the degenerate case essentially never triggers. Returning 0 is fine and consistent with Sharpe.

Actually, on reflection, returning 0 for "no downside" is BAD because it ranks a perfect strategy as worst. Let me return a large finite value (e.g., 10.0) for the no-downside case, which is high enough to rank well but won't break arithmetic. Or better: since the test data has all-positive returns (trend="up" in `_make_ohlcv`), the degenerate case WILL trigger in tests. So I need a sensible behavior.

Let me think about the actual semantics: in `_make_ohlcv(trend="up")`, close goes 100вҶ’130 monotonically up. The strategy signals (dual_ma crossover) will produce some buys and sells. The daily returns of the portfolio won't be all positive вҖ” there will be days where the position is flat (0 return) or slightly negative due to slippage/fees. So downside != 0 in practice.

But to be safe, let me handle it: return 0.0 when downside_dev == 0 (degenerate), with a clear comment. This matches the existing `_compute_sharpe` convention. If a real strategy has no downside, we can revisit. The Constitution wants conservative risk measurement, so returning 0 (rather than inf) is conservative.

Hmm, but actually for the portfolio_sortino aggregation, returning 0 for a no-downside strategy would drag down the average. Let me reconsider.

You know what вҖ” let me just use the standard convention and return inf-safe behavior:
```python
if dd <= 0 or np.isnan(dd):
    # ж— дёӢиЎҢжіўеҠЁ вҶ’ Sortino ж— е®ҡд№үпјҲзҗҶи®әдёә +infпјү
    # иҝ”еӣһ 0.0 дҝқжҢҒдёҺ _compute_sharpe дёҖиҮҙзҡ„йҖҖеҢ–иЎҢдёә
    return 0.0
```

This is the most conservative choice and matches the existing pattern. I'll document it clearly.

Now for the `_run_group` warning. Currently:
```python
def _backtest_one(df, strategy_name, params, ...):
    strategy_fn = STRATEGY_REGISTRY.get(strategy_name)
    if strategy_fn is None:
        return None  # silent
```

The issue is the None is returned silently. The caller `_run_group` sees `results` empty and logs "no valid results" at WARNING, but doesn't say WHY. 

Best fix: add an early check in `_run_group` BEFORE the param loop:
```python
for strategy in strategies:
    if strategy not in STRATEGY_REGISTRY:
        logger.warning(f"[MatrixBacktest] strategy '{strategy}' not in registry вҖ” skipped. "
                       f"Check strategy name spelling against @register_strategy decorators.")
        continue
    ...
```

This way the warning is at the point of detection, with the strategy name clearly identified. And it's logged ONCE per strategy (not once per symbol Г— param combo).

Now for the Sortino in the JSON output. Currently:
```python
weights_list.append({
    "strategy": strategy,
    "params": params,
    "weight": round(weight, 4),
    "backtest_sharpe": round(gr.portfolio_sharpe if gr else 0.0, 4),
    "backtest_win_rate": round(gr.avg_win_rate_pct / 100 if gr else 0.5, 4),
})
```

Add:
```python
    "backtest_sortino": round(gr.portfolio_sortino if gr else 0.0, 4),
```

Now let me implement. I'll make several edits to matrix_backtest.py:
1. Add `_compute_sortino()` function
2. Add `sortino: float = 0.0` to SingleBacktestResult
3. Add `portfolio_sortino: float = 0.0` to GroupBacktestResult
4. Add registry check + warning in `_run_group`
5. Compute sortino in `_backtest_one`
6. Add `_portfolio_sortino_from_results()`
7. Compute portfolio_sortino in `_run_group` for best_results
8. Add `backtest_sortino` to JSON output

Let me also check: `_optimize_ensemble_weights` uses `_portfolio_sharpe_from_results`. Should I switch it to Sortino? No вҖ” the Constitution says Sortino is the optimization target, but changing the weight optimization objective is a bigger decision. For now, I'll just ADD Sortino as a reported metric, not change the optimization objective. The weights still optimize on Sharpe (current behavior), but Sortino is reported so we can SEE it. Switching the optimization target is a separate (slightly higher-risk) decision that should be a separate iteration. I'll note this in the decision log.

Actually wait вҖ” re-reading Constitution L1: "йҰ–иҰҒ KPI: Sortino жҜ”зҺҮпјҲеңЁ DDвүӨ20% зәҰжқҹдёӢдјҳеҢ–пјү". This says Sortino is the optimization target. But changing the optimization from SharpeвҶ’Sortino in `_optimize_ensemble_weights` is a behavioral change that could shift weights significantly. 

Hmm. Let me be pragmatic: this iteration's PRIMARY goal is the bug fix. Adding Sortino as a REPORTED metric is clearly low-risk (just measurement). CHANGING the optimization objective from Sharpe to Sortino is a behavioral change вҖ” even if it aligns with Constitution, it's a separate decision that warrants its own iteration + verification. 

I'll add Sortino as a reported metric only, and note in the decision log that "switching optimization target to Sortino" is a candidate for the next iteration. This is the conservative, non-over-engineering approach.

Let me make the edits now.зҗҶи§ЈдәҶ `SingleBacktestResult` еңЁжөӢиҜ•йҮҢиў«дҪҚзҪ®ејҸжһ„йҖ пјҲ`SingleBacktestResult("SYM1", "s1", {}, s1, 10, 5, 60, 20, r1)`пјүпјҢж–°еӯ—ж®өеҝ…йЎ»еёҰ default еҠ еңЁжң«е°ҫгҖӮејҖе§Ӣж”№ `matrix_backtest.py`гҖӮ
